'use client';

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { useParams } from 'next/navigation';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type ImportJob = Database['public']['Tables']['import_jobs']['Row'];
type ImportJobRow = Database['public']['Tables']['import_job_rows']['Row'];

export default function ImportJobDetailPage() {
  const params = useParams();
  const id = params.id as string;

  const [job, setJob] = useState<ImportJob | null>(null);
  const [rows, setRows] = useState<ImportJobRow[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState<'all' | 'success' | 'error'>('all');

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      const [jobRes, rowsRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('import_jobs').select('*').eq('id', id).single(),
        supabase
          .from('import_job_rows')
          .select('*')
          .eq('import_job_id', id)
          .order('row_number', { ascending: true }),
      ]);
      setJob(jobRes.data);
      setRows(rowsRes.data ?? []);
      setLoading(false);
    }
    load();
  }, [id]);

  if (loading) {
    return <div className="p-4 text-sm text-gray-500">隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳ｭ...</div>;
  }

  if (!job) {
    return (
      <div className="p-4">
        <p className="text-sm text-red-600 mb-4">
          蜿冶ｾｼ繧ｸ繝ｧ繝悶′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・
        </p>
        <Link
          href="/admin/import"
          className="text-sm text-blue-600 hover:underline"
        >
          蜿冶ｾｼ邂｡逅・↓謌ｻ繧・
        </Link>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const d = new Date(job.created_at);
  const dateStr = `${d.getFullYear()}/${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}/${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')} ${String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}`;

  const filteredRows =
    filter === 'all' ? rows : rows.filter((r) => r.status === filter);
  const successCount = rows.filter((r) => r.status === 'success').length;
  const errorCount = rows.filter((r) => r.status === 'error').length;

  return (
    <div className="max-w-5xl">
      {/* 繝代Φ縺上★ */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4 text-sm">
        <Link
          href="/admin/import"
          className="text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700"
        >
          蜿冶ｾｼ邂｡逅・
        </Link>
        <span className="text-gray-300">/</span>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">蜿冶ｾｼ隧ｳ邏ｰ</h1>
      </div>

      {/* 讎りｦ・*/}
      <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-4 mb-4">
        <h2 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 mb-3">蜿冶ｾｼ讎りｦ・/h2>
        <dl className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-x-6 gap-y-2 text-sm">
          <dt className="text-gray-500">繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ蜷・/dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800 font-medium">{job.file_name}</dd>
          <dt className="text-gray-500">螳溯｡梧律譎・/dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800">{dateStr}</dd>
          <dt className="text-gray-500">螳溯｡瑚・/dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800">{job.executed_by}</dd>
          <dt className="text-gray-500">邱剰｡梧焚</dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800">{job.total_rows}陦・/dd>
        </dl>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 mt-4">
          <div className="p-3 border rounded text-center bg-green-50 border-green-200 text-green-800">
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold">{job.success_count}</p>
            <p className="text-xs mt-1">謌仙粥</p>
          </div>
          <div className="p-3 border rounded text-center bg-red-50 border-red-200 text-red-800">
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold">{job.error_count}</p>
            <p className="text-xs mt-1">螟ｱ謨・/p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 繝輔ぅ繝ｫ繧ｿ繝ｼ */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
        <FilterButton
          label={`縺吶∋縺ｦ (${rows.length})`}
          active={filter === 'all'}
          onClick={() => setFilter('all')}
        />
        <FilterButton
          label={`謌仙粥 (${successCount})`}
          active={filter === 'success'}
          onClick={() => setFilter('success')}
        />
        <FilterButton
          label={`繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ (${errorCount})`}
          active={filter === 'error'}
          onClick={() => setFilter('error')}
        />
      </div>

      {/* 陦後ユ繝ｼ繝悶Ν */}
      <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded overflow-hidden">
        <table className="w-full text-sm">
          <thead>
            <tr className="bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-200">
              <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 w-16">
                陦・
              </th>
              <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 w-20">
                迥ｶ諷・
              </th>
              <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700">
                蜀・ｮｹ
              </th>
              <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700">
                繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ逅・罰
              </th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            {filteredRows.map((row) => {
              const rawData = row.raw_data_json as Record<string, unknown>;
              const userName = (rawData.userName ??
                rawData['莠育ｴ・・錐'] ??
                '') as string;
              const siteNumber = (rawData.siteNumber ??
                rawData['繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ'] ??
                '') as string;
              const checkIn = (rawData.checkInDate ??
                rawData['繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･'] ??
                '') as string;

              return (
                <tr key={row.id} className="border-b border-gray-100">
                  <td className="px-3 py-2 text-gray-500">
                    {row.row_number}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-2">
                    {row.status === 'success' ? (
                      <span className="inline-block px-1.5 py-0.5 text-xs rounded bg-green-100 text-green-700">
                        謌仙粥
                      </span>
                    ) : (
                      <span className="inline-block px-1.5 py-0.5 text-xs rounded bg-red-100 text-red-700">
                        繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-2 text-xs text-gray-800">
                    {userName && <span>{userName}</span>}
                    {siteNumber && (
                      <span className="ml-2 text-gray-500">
                        繧ｵ繧､繝・{siteNumber}
                      </span>
                    )}
                    {checkIn && (
                      <span className="ml-2 text-gray-500">{checkIn}</span>
                    )}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-2 text-xs text-red-600">
                    {row.error_message || '-'}
                  </td>
                </tr>
              );
            })}
            {filteredRows.length === 0 && (
              <tr>
                <td
                  colSpan={4}
                  className="px-3 py-6 text-center text-gray-400 text-sm"
                >
                  隧ｲ蠖薙☆繧玖｡後′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・
                </td>
              </tr>
            )}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function FilterButton({
  label,
  active,
  onClick,
}: {
  label: string;
  active: boolean;
  onClick: () => void;
}) {
  return (
    <button
      onClick={onClick}
      className={`px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded border transition-colors ${
        active
          ? 'bg-gray-900 text-white border-gray-900'
          : 'bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-50'
      }`}
    >
      {label}
    </button>
  );
}

'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { useImportHistoryStore } from '@/stores/importHistoryStore';
import type { ImportHistoryEntry, ImportHistoryError } from '@/types/importHistory';

export default function ImportHistoryPage() {
  const entries = useImportHistoryStore((s) => s.entries);
  const clearAll = useImportHistoryStore((s) => s.clearAll);
  const [selectedId, setSelectedId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [confirmClear, setConfirmClear] = useState(false);

  const selected = selectedId
    ? entries.find((e) => e.id === selectedId) ?? null
    : null;

  return (
    <div className="max-w-5xl">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">蜿冶ｾｼ螻･豁ｴ</h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
            繧ｹ繝励Ξ繝・ラ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝亥叙霎ｼ縺ｮ螳溯｡悟ｱ･豁ｴ縺ｨ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧堤｢ｺ隱阪〒縺阪∪縺吶・
          </p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <Link
            href="/admin/import"
            className="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-50"
          >
            蜿冶ｾｼ逕ｻ髱｢縺ｸ
          </Link>
          {entries.length > 0 && (
            confirmClear ? (
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <button
                  onClick={() => { clearAll(); setConfirmClear(false); setSelectedId(null); }}
                  className="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white bg-red-600 rounded hover:bg-red-700"
                >
                  蜑企勁縺吶ｋ
                </button>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setConfirmClear(false)}
                  className="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-50"
                >
                  繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ
                </button>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <button
                onClick={() => setConfirmClear(true)}
                className="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-red-600 bg-white border border-red-200 rounded hover:bg-red-50"
              >
                蜈ｨ螻･豁ｴ蜑企勁
              </button>
            )
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {entries.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-8 text-center">
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">蜿冶ｾｼ螻･豁ｴ縺ｯ縺ｾ縺縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・/p>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="flex gap-4">
          {/* 蟾ｦ: 螻･豁ｴ荳隕ｧ */}
          <div className="w-80 shrink-0 space-y-2">
            {entries.map((entry) => (
              <HistoryCard
                key={entry.id}
                entry={entry}
                isSelected={entry.id === selectedId}
                onClick={() => setSelectedId(entry.id === selectedId ? null : entry.id)}
              />
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* 蜿ｳ: 隧ｳ邏ｰ */}
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
            {selected ? (
              <HistoryDetail entry={selected} />
            ) : (
              <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-8 text-center">
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">
                  蟾ｦ縺ｮ螻･豁ｴ繧帝∈謚槭☆繧九→隧ｳ邏ｰ縺瑚｡ｨ遉ｺ縺輔ｌ縺ｾ縺吶・

// 笏笏笏 繧ｵ繝悶さ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・笏笏笏

function HistoryCard({
  entry,
  isSelected,
  onClick,
}: {
  entry: ImportHistoryEntry;
  isSelected: boolean;
  onClick: () => void;
}) {
  const d = new Date(entry.executedAt);
  const dateStr = `${d.getFullYear()}/${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}/${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')} ${String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
  const hasErrors = entry.failedCount > 0 || entry.validationErrorCount > 0 || entry.duplicateCount > 0;

  return (
    <button
      onClick={onClick}
      className={`w-full text-left p-3 rounded border transition-colors ${
        isSelected
          ? 'bg-gray-50 border-gray-400'
          : 'bg-white border-gray-200 hover:border-gray-300'
      }`}
    >
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1">
        <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">{dateStr}</span>
        {hasErrors ? (
          <span className="text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-red-100 text-red-700">
            繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺ゅｊ
          </span>
        ) : (
          <span className="text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-green-100 text-green-700">
            豁｣蟶ｸ
          </span>
        )}
      </div>
      <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 truncate">{entry.fileName}</p>
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500">
        <span>謌仙粥 {entry.insertedCount}</span>
        {entry.failedCount > 0 && (
          <span className="text-red-600">螟ｱ謨・{entry.failedCount}</span>
        )}
        {entry.validationErrorCount > 0 && (
          <span className="text-red-600">讀懆ｨｼNG {entry.validationErrorCount}</span>
        )}
        {entry.duplicateCount > 0 && (
          <span className="text-yellow-600">驥崎､・{entry.duplicateCount}</span>
        )}
      </div>
      <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1 truncate">{entry.executedBy}</p>
    </button>
  );
}

function HistoryDetail({ entry }: { entry: ImportHistoryEntry }) {
  const d = new Date(entry.executedAt);
  const dateStr = `${d.getFullYear()}蟷ｴ${d.getMonth() + 1}譛・{d.getDate()}譌･ ${String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(d.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0')}`;

  const validationErrors = entry.errors.filter((e) => e.phase === 'validation');
  const duplicateErrors = entry.errors.filter((e) => e.phase === 'duplicate');
  const insertErrors = entry.errors.filter((e) => e.phase === 'insert');

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* 蝓ｺ譛ｬ諠・ｱ */}
      <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-4">
        <h2 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 mb-3">蜿冶ｾｼ讎りｦ・/h2>
        <dl className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-x-4 gap-y-2 text-sm">
          <dt className="text-gray-500">繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ蜷・/dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800 font-medium">{entry.fileName}</dd>
          <dt className="text-gray-500">螳溯｡梧律譎・/dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800">{dateStr}</dd>
          <dt className="text-gray-500">螳溯｡瑚・/dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800">{entry.executedBy}</dd>
          <dt className="text-gray-500">邱剰｡梧焚</dt>
          <dd className="text-gray-800">{entry.totalRows}陦・/dd>
        </dl>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-3 mt-4">
          <MiniCard label="蜿冶ｾｼ謌仙粥" count={entry.insertedCount} color="green" />
          <MiniCard label="INSERT螟ｱ謨・ count={entry.failedCount} color="red" />
          <MiniCard label="讀懆ｨｼNG繧ｹ繧ｭ繝・・" count={entry.validationErrorCount} color="red" />
          <MiniCard label="驥崎､・せ繧ｭ繝・・" count={entry.duplicateCount} color="yellow" />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ辟｡縺・*/}
      {entry.errors.length === 0 && (
        <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded p-4 text-center">
          <p className="text-sm text-green-700">縺吶∋縺ｦ縺ｮ陦後′豁｣蟶ｸ縺ｫ蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｾ繧後∪縺励◆縲・/p>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ */}
      {validationErrors.length > 0 && (
        <ErrorSection
          title="繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ"
          description="繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ讀懆ｨｼ谿ｵ髫弱〒髯､螟悶＆繧後◆陦後〒縺吶ょ叙霎ｼ縺ｯ隧ｦ陦後＆繧後※縺・∪縺帙ｓ縲・
          errors={validationErrors}
          color="red"
        />
      )}

      {/* 驥崎､・お繝ｩ繝ｼ */}
      {duplicateErrors.length > 0 && (
        <ErrorSection
          title="驥崎､・せ繧ｭ繝・・"
          description="譌｢蟄倅ｺ育ｴ・∪縺溘・繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ蜀・・蛻･陦後→譌･遞九′驥崎､・＠縺ｦ縺・◆縺溘ａ髯､螟悶＆繧後◆陦後〒縺吶・
          errors={duplicateErrors}
          color="yellow"
        />
      )}

      {/* INSERT螟ｱ謨・*/}
      {insertErrors.length > 0 && (
        <ErrorSection
          title="INSERT螟ｱ謨・
          description="繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ騾夐℃蠕後√ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ繝吶・繧ｹ縺ｸ縺ｮ譖ｸ縺崎ｾｼ縺ｿ譎ゅ↓繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺溯｡後〒縺吶・
          errors={insertErrors}
          color="red"
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function ErrorSection({
  title,
  description,
  errors,
  color,
}: {
  title: string;
  description: string;
  errors: ImportHistoryError[];
  color: 'red' | 'yellow';
}) {
  const borderColor = color === 'red' ? 'border-red-200' : 'border-yellow-200';
  const bgColor = color === 'red' ? 'bg-red-50' : 'bg-yellow-50';
  const titleColor = color === 'red' ? 'text-red-700' : 'text-yellow-700';
  const textColor = color === 'red' ? 'text-red-600' : 'text-yellow-600';
  const rowBg = color === 'red' ? 'bg-red-50 border-red-100' : 'bg-yellow-50 border-yellow-100';

  return (
    <div className={`bg-white border ${borderColor} rounded p-4`}>
      <h3 className={`text-sm font-medium ${titleColor} mb-1`}>
        {title}・・errors.length}莉ｶ・・
      </h3>
      <p className={`text-xs ${textColor} mb-3`}>{description}</p>
      <div className="space-y-2 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto">
        {errors.map((err, i) => (
          <div
            key={i}
            className={`p-2 ${rowBg} border rounded text-xs`}
          >
            <p className={`font-medium ${color === 'red' ? 'text-red-800' : 'text-yellow-800'} mb-1`}>
              陦・{err.rowIndex}: {err.userName} / 繧ｵ繧､繝・{err.siteNumber}
            </p>
            <ul className={`list-disc list-inside ${textColor} space-y-0.5`}>
              {err.reasons.map((r, j) => (
                <li key={j}>{r}</li>
              ))}
            </ul>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function MiniCard({
  label,
  count,
  color,
}: {
  label: string;
  count: number;
  color: 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow';
}) {
  const styles = {
    green: 'bg-green-50 border-green-200 text-green-800',
    red: 'bg-red-50 border-red-200 text-red-800',
    yellow: 'bg-yellow-50 border-yellow-200 text-yellow-800',
  };

  return (
    <div className={`p-2 border rounded text-center ${styles[color]}`}>
      <p className="text-lg font-bold">{count}</p>
      <p className="text-[10px] mt-0.5 leading-tight">{label}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

'use client';

import { useState, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';

  parseFileToRows,

  validateAllRows,
} from '@/lib/admin/importParser';

  ImportParsedRow,
  ImportRowError,
  ImportDuplicate,
  ImportExecutionResult,
} from '@/types/import';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type Step = 'upload' | 'validate' | 'result';
type ImportJob = Database['public']['Tables']['import_jobs']['Row'];

export default function AdminImportPage() {

  const [fileName, setFileName] = useState('');
  const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false);

  const [validRows, setValidRows] = useState<ImportParsedRow[]>([]);
  const [errorRows, setErrorRows] = useState<ImportRowError[]>([]);
  const [duplicateRows, setDuplicateRows] = useState<ImportDuplicate[]>([]);
  const [parseError, setParseError] = useState('');

  // 蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ邨先棡
  const [execResult, setExecResult] = useState<ImportExecutionResult | null>(
    null,
  );

  // 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ繧｢繝・・繝ｭ繝ｼ繝牙・逅・
  const handleFileUpload = useCallback(
    async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
      const file = e.target.files?.[0];
      if (!file) return;

      setParseError('');
      setIsProcessing(true);
      setFileName(file.name);

      try {
        const buffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
        const { rows, error } = parseFileToRows(buffer, file.name);

        if (error) {
          setParseError(error);
          setIsProcessing(false);
          return;
        }

        if (rows.length === 0) {
          setParseError('繝・・繧ｿ陦後′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ');
          setIsProcessing(false);
          return;
        }

        // 繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ繝√ぉ繝・け
        const headers = Object.keys(rows[0]);
        const { ok, missing } = checkRequiredColumns(headers);
        if (!ok) {
          setParseError(
            `蠢・亥・縺御ｸ崎ｶｳ縺励※縺・∪縺・ ${missing.join(', ')}`,
          );
          setIsProcessing(false);
          return;
        }

        // 繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ繧担upabase縺九ｉ蜿門ｾ・
        let siteNumbers: string[] | undefined;
        const { data: sitesData } = await supabase
          .from('sites')
          .select('site_number')
          .eq('is_active', true);

        // sites繝・・繝悶Ν縺ｫ繝・・繧ｿ縺後≠繧句ｴ蜷医・縺昴ｌ繧貞茜逕ｨ
        if (sitesData && sitesData.length > 0) {
          siteNumbers = sitesData.map((s) => s.site_number);
        }
        // 繝・・繧ｿ縺後↑縺・ｴ蜷医・繝繝溘・縺ｮ繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ繝ｪ繧ｹ繝医↓繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ

        // 譌｢蟄倅ｺ育ｴ・ｒ蜿門ｾ暦ｼ磯㍾隍・メ繧ｧ繝・け逕ｨ・・
        const { data: existingData } = await supabase
          .from('guest_reservations')
          .select('site_number, check_in_date, check_out_date')
          .not('status', 'eq', 'cancelled');

        const existing = (existingData ?? []).map((r) => ({
          site_number: r.site_number ?? '',
          check_in_date: r.check_in_date,
          check_out_date: r.check_out_date,
        }));

        // 繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ
        const result = validateAllRows(rows, existing, siteNumbers);
        setValidRows(result.validRows);
        setErrorRows(result.errorRows);
        setDuplicateRows(result.duplicateRows);
        setStep('validate');
      } catch {
        setParseError('繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ縺ｮ蜃ｦ逅・ｸｭ縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺ｾ縺励◆');
      } finally {
        setIsProcessing(false);
      }
    },
    [],
  );

  // 蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ螳溯｡・
  const handleExecute = useCallback(async () => {
    if (validRows.length === 0) return;

    setIsProcessing(true);
    try {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();

      const res = await fetch('/api/import-reservations', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          rows: validRows,
          errorRows,
          duplicateRows,
          fileName,
          executedBy: user?.email ?? '荳肴・',
        }),
      });

      if (!res.ok) {
        const body = await res.json();
        setParseError(body.error ?? '蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆');
        return;
      }

      const result: ImportExecutionResult = await res.json();
      setExecResult(result);
      setStep('result');
      fetchHistory();
    } catch {
      setParseError('蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ蜃ｦ逅・ｸｭ縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺ｾ縺励◆');
    } finally {
      setIsProcessing(false);
    }
  }, [validRows, errorRows, duplicateRows, fileName]);

  // 繝ｪ繧ｻ繝・ヨ
  const handleReset = useCallback(() => {
    setStep('upload');
    setFileName('');
    setValidRows([]);
    setErrorRows([]);
    setDuplicateRows([]);
    setParseError('');
    setExecResult(null);
  }, []);

  // 螻･豁ｴ
  const [historyJobs, setHistoryJobs] = useState<ImportJob[]>([]);

  const fetchHistory = useCallback(async () => {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('import_jobs')
      .select('*')
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(20);
    if (data) setHistoryJobs(data);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchHistory();
  }, [fetchHistory]);

  return (
    <div className="max-w-5xl">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-4">
        莠育ｴ・ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ蜿冶ｾｼ
      </h1>
      <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-6">
        CSV 縺ｾ縺溘・ Excel 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ縺九ｉ莠育ｴ・ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ繧剃ｸ諡ｬ逋ｻ骭ｲ縺励∪縺吶・
      </p>

      {/* 繧ｹ繝・ャ繝励う繝ｳ繧ｸ繧ｱ繝ｼ繧ｿ繝ｼ */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-6 text-xs text-gray-500">
        <StepBadge label="1. 繧｢繝・・繝ｭ繝ｼ繝・ active={step === 'upload'} done={step !== 'upload'} />
        <span>/</span>
        <StepBadge label="2. 讀懆ｨｼ" active={step === 'validate'} done={step === 'result'} />
        <span>/</span>
        <StepBadge label="3. 邨先棡" active={step === 'result'} done={false} />
      </div>

      {parseError && (
        <div className="mb-4 p-3 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded text-sm text-red-700">
          {parseError}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Step 1: 繧｢繝・・繝ｭ繝ｼ繝・*/}
      {step === 'upload' && (
        <UploadStep
          isProcessing={isProcessing}
          onFileChange={handleFileUpload}
        />
      )}

      {/* Step 2: 讀懆ｨｼ邨先棡 */}
      {step === 'validate' && (
        <ValidateStep
          fileName={fileName}
          validRows={validRows}
          errorRows={errorRows}
          duplicateRows={duplicateRows}
          isProcessing={isProcessing}
          onExecute={handleExecute}
          onReset={handleReset}
        />
      )}

      {/* Step 3: 蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ邨先棡 */}
      {step === 'result' && execResult && (
        <ResultStep result={execResult} onReset={handleReset} />
      )}

      {/* 蜿冶ｾｼ螻･豁ｴ */}
      <HistorySection jobs={historyJobs} />
    </div>
  );
}

// --- 繧ｵ繝悶さ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・---

function StepBadge({
  label,
  active,
  done,
}: {
  label: string;
  active: boolean;
  done: boolean;
}) {
  return (
    <span
      className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded ${
        active
          ? 'bg-gray-900 text-white font-medium'
          : done
            ? 'bg-gray-200 text-gray-600'
            : 'text-gray-400'
      }`}
    >
      {label}
    </span>
  );
}

function UploadStep({
  isProcessing,
  onFileChange,
}: {
  isProcessing: boolean;
  onFileChange: (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => void;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-6">
        <h2 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 mb-3">
          繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ驕ｸ謚・
        </h2>
        <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-4">
          蟇ｾ蠢懷ｽ｢蠑・ .csv, .xlsx, .xls
        </p>
        <label className="block">
          <input
            type="file"
            accept=".csv,.xlsx,.xls"
            onChange={onFileChange}
            disabled={isProcessing}
            className="block w-full text-sm text-gray-500
              file:mr-4 file:py-2 file:px-4
              file:rounded file:border file:border-gray-300
              file:text-sm file:font-medium
              file:bg-white file:text-gray-700
              hover:file:bg-gray-50
              disabled:opacity-50"
          />
        </label>
        {isProcessing && (
          <p className="mt-3 text-sm text-gray-500">繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ繧呈､懆ｨｼ荳ｭ...</p>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-6">
        <h2 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 mb-3">
          繝・Φ繝励Ξ繝ｼ繝亥・
        </h2>
        <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-3">
          莉･荳九・蛻励ｒ繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ陦後↓蜷ｫ繧√※縺上□縺輔＞縲・
        </p>
        <div className="overflow-x-auto">
          <table className="w-full text-xs border border-gray-200">
            <thead>
              <tr className="bg-gray-50">
                <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b border-gray-200">
                  蛻怜錐
                </th>
                <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b border-gray-200">
                  蠢・・
                </th>
                <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b border-gray-200">
                  蠖｢蠑・
                </th>
                <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b border-gray-200">
                  萓・
                </th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {TEMPLATE_COLUMNS.map((col) => (
                <tr key={col.name} className="border-b border-gray-100">
                  <td className="px-3 py-1.5 font-mono text-gray-800">
                    {col.name}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-1.5 text-gray-600">
                    {col.required ? '蠢・・ : '莉ｻ諢・}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-1.5 text-gray-500">{col.format}</td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-1.5 text-gray-500">{col.example}</td>
                </tr>
              ))}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function ValidateStep({
  fileName,
  validRows,
  errorRows,
  duplicateRows,
  isProcessing,
  onExecute,
  onReset,
}: {
  fileName: string;
  validRows: ImportParsedRow[];
  errorRows: ImportRowError[];
  duplicateRows: ImportDuplicate[];
  isProcessing: boolean;
  onExecute: () => void;
  onReset: () => void;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* 繧ｵ繝槭Μ繝ｼ */}
      <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-4">
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-3">
          繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ: <span className="font-medium text-gray-800">{fileName}</span>
        </p>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
          <SummaryCard label="豁｣蟶ｸ" count={validRows.length} color="green" />
          <SummaryCard label="繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ" count={errorRows.length} color="red" />
          <SummaryCard
            label="驥崎､・呵｣・
            count={duplicateRows.length}
            color="yellow"
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 豁｣蟶ｸ陦後・繝ｬ繝薙Η繝ｼ */}
      {validRows.length > 0 && (
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-4">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 mb-3">
            蜿冶ｾｼ蟇ｾ雎｡: {validRows.length}莉ｶ
          </h3>
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="w-full text-xs border border-gray-200">
              <thead>
                <tr className="bg-gray-50">
                  <th className="px-2 py-1.5 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b">
                    陦・
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1.5 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b">
                    莠育ｴ・・錐
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1.5 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b">
                    繧ｵ繧､繝・
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1.5 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b">
                    繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1.5 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b">
                    繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝・
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1.5 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b">
                    莠ｺ謨ｰ
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1.5 text-left font-medium text-gray-700 border-b">
                    謾ｯ謇輔＞
                  </th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                {validRows.map((row) => (
                  <tr key={row.rowIndex} className="border-b border-gray-100">
                    <td className="px-2 py-1.5 text-gray-500">
                      {row.rowIndex}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1.5 text-gray-800">
                      {row.userName}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1.5 text-gray-800">
                      {row.siteNumber}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1.5 text-gray-600">
                      {row.checkInDate}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1.5 text-gray-600">
                      {row.checkOutDate}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1.5 text-gray-600">
                      {row.guests}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1.5 text-gray-600">
                      {row.paymentMethod}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ陦・*/}
      {errorRows.length > 0 && (
        <div className="bg-white border border-red-200 rounded p-4">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-red-700 mb-3">
            繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ: {errorRows.length}莉ｶ
          </h3>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {errorRows.map((row) => (
              <div
                key={row.rowIndex}
                className="p-2 bg-red-50 border border-red-100 rounded text-xs"
              >
                <p className="font-medium text-red-800 mb-1">
                  陦・{row.rowIndex}: {row.raw.莠育ｴ・・錐 || '(蜷榊燕縺ｪ縺・'} /
                  繧ｵ繧､繝・{row.raw.繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ || '(譛ｪ險ｭ螳・'}
                </p>
                <ul className="list-disc list-inside text-red-600 space-y-0.5">
                  {row.errors.map((err, i) => (
                    <li key={i}>{err}</li>
                  ))}
                </ul>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 驥崎､・呵｣・*/}
      {duplicateRows.length > 0 && (
        <div className="bg-white border border-yellow-200 rounded p-4">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-yellow-700 mb-3">
            驥崎､・呵｣・ {duplicateRows.length}莉ｶ
          </h3>
          <p className="text-xs text-yellow-600 mb-2">
            莉･荳九・陦後・蜷御ｸ繧ｵ繧､繝医・蜷御ｸ譛滄俣縺ｫ譌｢蟄倅ｺ育ｴ・∪縺溘・繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ蜀・・蛻･陦後→驥崎､・＠縺ｦ縺・∪縺吶ょ叙霎ｼ蟇ｾ雎｡縺九ｉ髯､螟悶＆繧後∪縺吶・
          </p>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {duplicateRows.map((dup) => (
              <div
                key={dup.rowIndex}
                className="p-2 bg-yellow-50 border border-yellow-100 rounded text-xs"
              >
                <p className="text-yellow-800">
                  陦・{dup.rowIndex}: {dup.parsed.userName} / 繧ｵ繧､繝・' '}
                  {dup.parsed.siteNumber} / {dup.parsed.checkInDate} 縲悳' '}
                  {dup.parsed.checkOutDate}
                </p>
                <p className="text-yellow-600">
                  譌｢蟄・ {dup.existingCheckIn} 縲・{dup.existingCheckOut}
                </p>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 繧｢繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <button
          onClick={onExecute}
          disabled={isProcessing || validRows.length === 0}
          className="px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white bg-gray-900 rounded hover:bg-gray-800 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed"
        >
          {isProcessing
            ? '蜿冶ｾｼ荳ｭ...'
            : `${validRows.length}莉ｶ繧貞叙繧願ｾｼ繧`}
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={onReset}
          disabled={isProcessing}
          className="px-4 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-50 disabled:opacity-40"
        >
          繧・ｊ逶ｴ縺・
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function ResultStep({
  result,
  onReset,
}: {
  result: ImportExecutionResult;
  onReset: () => void;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-6">
        <h2 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-800 mb-4">
          蜿冶ｾｼ邨先棡
        </h2>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 mb-4">
          <SummaryCard
            label="蜿冶ｾｼ謌仙粥"
            count={result.insertedCount}
            color="green"
          />
          <SummaryCard
            label="蜿冶ｾｼ螟ｱ謨・
            count={result.failedCount}
            color="red"
          />
        </div>

        {result.failures.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-4">
            <h3 className="text-xs font-medium text-red-700 mb-2">
              螟ｱ謨励＠縺溯｡・
            </h3>
            <div className="space-y-1">
              {result.failures.map((f, i) => (
                <p key={i} className="text-xs text-red-600">
                  陦・{f.rowIndex}: {f.error}
                </p>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <button
          onClick={onReset}
          className="px-4 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-50"
        >
          蛻･縺ｮ繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ繧貞叙繧願ｾｼ繧
        </button>
        {result.jobId && (
          <Link
            href={`/admin/import/${result.jobId}`}
            className="px-4 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-50"
          >
            蜿冶ｾｼ隧ｳ邏ｰ繧定ｦ九ｋ
          </Link>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function SummaryCard({
  label,
  count,
  color,
}: {
  label: string;
  count: number;
  color: 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow';
}) {
  const styles = {
    green: 'bg-green-50 border-green-200 text-green-800',
    red: 'bg-red-50 border-red-200 text-red-800',
    yellow: 'bg-yellow-50 border-yellow-200 text-yellow-800',
  };

  return (
    <div className={`p-3 border rounded text-center ${styles[color]}`}>
      <p className="text-2xl font-bold">{count}</p>
      <p className="text-xs mt-1">{label}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

  {
    name: '莠育ｴ・・錐',
    required: true,
    format: '繝・く繧ｹ繝・,
    example: '螻ｱ逕ｰ螟ｪ驛・,
  },
  {
    name: '髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ',
    required: true,
    format: '繝・く繧ｹ繝・,
    example: '090-1234-5678',
  },
  {
    name: '繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ',
    required: true,
    format: '繝・く繧ｹ繝・,
    example: 'yamada@example.com',
  },
  {
    name: '繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･',
    required: true,
    format: 'YYYY-MM-DD 縺ｾ縺溘・ YYYY/MM/DD',
    example: '2026-05-01',
  },
  {
    name: '繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律',
    required: true,
    format: 'YYYY-MM-DD 縺ｾ縺溘・ YYYY/MM/DD',
    example: '2026-05-03',
  },
  {
    name: '莠ｺ謨ｰ',
    required: true,
    format: '謨ｴ謨ｰ・・莉･荳奇ｼ・,
    example: '4',
  },
  {
    name: '繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ',
    required: true,
    format: '繝・く繧ｹ繝・,
    example: 'A-01',
  },
  {

'use client';

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useRouter, useSearchParams } from 'next/navigation';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';

export default function AdminLoginPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();

  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  // URL 繝代Λ繝｡繝ｼ繧ｿ縺九ｉ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ繧貞叙蠕・
  useEffect(() => {
    const errParam = searchParams.get('error');
    if (errParam === 'forbidden') {
      setError('邂｡逅・・ｨｩ髯舌′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲らｮ｡逅・・い繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝医〒繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ縺励※縺上□縺輔＞縲・);
    }
  }, [searchParams]);

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError(null);
    setLoading(true);

    try {
      const { error: authError } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
        email: email.trim(),
        password,
      });

      if (authError) {
        if (authError.message.includes('Invalid login credentials')) {
          setError('繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ縺ｾ縺溘・繝代せ繝ｯ繝ｼ繝峨′豁｣縺励￥縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・);
        } else {
          setError(authError.message);
        }
        setLoading(false);
        return;
      }

      // 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ謌仙粥 竊・middleware 縺檎ｮ｡逅・・愛螳壹☆繧九・縺ｧ /admin 縺ｸ
      const next = searchParams.get('next') ?? '/admin';
      router.push(next);
      router.refresh();
    } catch {
      setError('繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ荳ｭ縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲・);
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-100 px-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-gray-200 p-8">
          {/* 繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ */}
          <div className="text-center mb-8">
            <div className="mx-auto mb-3 flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-gray-900">
              <svg
                className="h-6 w-6 text-white"
                fill="none"
                viewBox="0 0 24 24"
                stroke="currentColor"
                strokeWidth={2}
              >
                <path
                  strokeLinecap="round"
                  strokeLinejoin="round"
                  d="M12 15v2m-6 4h12a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2zm10-10V7a4 4 0 00-8 0v4h8z"
                />
              </svg>
            </div>
            <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">邂｡逅・判髱｢繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ</h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
              邂｡逅・・い繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝医〒繧ｵ繧､繝ｳ繧､繝ｳ縺励※縺上□縺輔＞
            </p>
          </div>

          {/* 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ */}
          {error && (
            <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg bg-red-50 border border-red-200 p-3">
              <p className="text-sm text-red-700">{error}</p>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 繝輔か繝ｼ繝 */}
          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
            <div>
              <label
                htmlFor="email"
                className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1"
              >
                繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ
              </label>
              <input
                id="email"
                type="email"
                required
                autoComplete="email"
                value={email}
                onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full rounded-lg border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:border-gray-900 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gray-900"
                placeholder="admin@example.com"
              />
            </div>

            <div>
              <label
                htmlFor="password"
                className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1"
              >
                繝代せ繝ｯ繝ｼ繝・
              </label>
              <input
                id="password"
                type="password"
                required
                autoComplete="current-password"
                value={password}
                onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full rounded-lg border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:border-gray-900 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gray-900"
                placeholder="窶｢窶｢窶｢窶｢窶｢窶｢窶｢窶｢"
              />
            </div>

              type="submit"

            </button>
          </form>
        </div>

          &copy; 繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ邂｡逅・す繧ｹ繝・Β
        </p>

  );

                <th className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-gray-600 font-medium">莠育ｴ・/th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {notifications.map((n) => (
                <tr key={n.id} className="border-b border-gray-50 hover:bg-gray-50">
                  <td className="px-3 py-2 text-gray-500 whitespace-nowrap">
                    {new Date(n.created_at).toLocaleString('ja-JP')}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-2 text-gray-800">
                    {getNotificationTypeLabel(n.notification_type)}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-3 py-2 text-gray-600">
                    {getChannelLabel(n.channel)}
                  </td>

function StatusBadge({ status }: { status: string }) {
  const label = getNotificationStatusLabel(status);
  const cls =
    status === 'sent'
      ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700'
      : status === 'failed'
        ? 'bg-red-100 text-red-700'
        : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600';

  return (
    <span className={`inline-block px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-xs ${cls}`}>
      {label}
    </span>
  );
}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import { fetchRecentActions, getActionLabel } from '@/lib/admin/actionLog';
import {
  fetchRecentNotifications,
  getNotificationTypeLabel,
  getChannelLabel,
  getNotificationStatusLabel,
} from '@/lib/admin/notificationLog';
import { dummySites, dummySalesRule } from '@/data/adminDummyData';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type ImportJob = Database['public']['Tables']['import_jobs']['Row'];
type ActionLog = Database['public']['Tables']['admin_action_logs']['Row'];
type NotificationLog = Database['public']['Tables']['notification_logs']['Row'];

interface DashboardStats {
  todayCheckins: number;
  next7DaysReservations: number;
  unpaidCount: number;
  cancelledCount: number;
}

function toDateStr(d: Date): string {
  return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
}

export default function AdminDashboardPage() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<DashboardStats | null>(null);
  const [recentImports, setRecentImports] = useState<ImportJob[]>([]);
  const [recentActions, setRecentActions] = useState<ActionLog[]>([]);
  const [recentNotifications, setRecentNotifications] = useState<NotificationLog[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      const today = new Date();
      const todayStr = toDateStr(today);
      const next7 = new Date(today);
      next7.setDate(next7.getDate() + 7);
      const next7Str = toDateStr(next7);

      const [
        { count: todayCheckins },
        { count: next7Days },
        { count: unpaid },
        { count: cancelled },
        { data: imports },
        actions,
        notifications,
      ] = await Promise.all([
        supabase
          .from('guest_reservations')
          .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true })
          .eq('check_in_date', todayStr)
          .not('status', 'eq', 'cancelled'),
        supabase
          .from('guest_reservations')
          .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true })
          .gte('check_in_date', todayStr)
          .lte('check_in_date', next7Str)
          .not('status', 'eq', 'cancelled'),
        supabase
          .from('guest_reservations')
          .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true })
          .eq('payment_status', 'pending')
          .not('status', 'eq', 'cancelled'),
        supabase
          .from('guest_reservations')
          .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true })
          .eq('status', 'cancelled'),
        supabase
          .from('import_jobs')
          .select('*')
          .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
          .limit(5),
        fetchRecentActions(5),
        fetchRecentNotifications(5),
      ]);

      setStats({
        todayCheckins: todayCheckins ?? 0,
        next7DaysReservations: next7Days ?? 0,
        unpaidCount: unpaid ?? 0,
        cancelledCount: cancelled ?? 0,
      });
      setRecentImports(imports ?? []);
      setRecentActions(actions);
      setRecentNotifications(notifications);
      setLoading(false);
    }
    load();
  }, []);

  // 蜿嶺ｻ伜●豁｢荳ｭ繧ｵ繧､繝・
  const closedSites = dummySites.filter((s) => s.status !== 'active');
  const hasClosedDates = dummySalesRule.closedDates.length > 0;
  const hasSiteClosures = dummySalesRule.siteClosures.length > 0;

  return (
    <div className="max-w-5xl">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-4">繝繝・す繝･繝懊・繝・/h1>

      {loading ? (
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳ｭ...</p>
      ) : (
        <>
          {/* 髮・ｨ医き繝ｼ繝・*/}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-6">
            <StatCard label="譛ｬ譌･縺ｮ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ" value={stats?.todayCheckins ?? 0} />
            <StatCard label="莉雁ｾ・譌･莉･蜀・・莠育ｴ・ value={stats?.next7DaysReservations ?? 0} />
            <StatCard label="譛ｪ豎ｺ貂・ value={stats?.unpaidCount ?? 0} color={stats?.unpaidCount ? 'yellow' : undefined} />
            <StatCard label="繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ" value={stats?.cancelledCount ?? 0} color={stats?.cancelledCount ? 'red' : undefined} />
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
            {/* 逶ｴ霑代・蜿冶ｾｼ螻･豁ｴ */}
            <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-800">逶ｴ霑代・蜿冶ｾｼ</h2>
                <Link href="/admin/import" className="text-xs text-blue-600 hover:underline">荳隕ｧ</Link>
              </div>
              {recentImports.length === 0 ? (
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">蜿冶ｾｼ螻･豁ｴ縺ｪ縺・/p>
              ) : (
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {recentImports.map((job) => (

                      href={`/admin/import/${job.id}`}
                      className="block p-2 rounded border border-gray-100 hover:bg-gray-50 text-xs"
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <span className="text-gray-800 font-medium truncate max-w-[160px]">{job.file_name}</span>
                        <span className="text-gray-400">{new Date(job.created_at).toLocaleDateString('ja-JP')}</span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex gap-3 mt-1 text-gray-500">
                        <span>謌仙粥 {job.success_count}</span>

                      {getChannelLabel(n.channel)}
                    </span>

                      {getNotificationStatusLabel(n.status)}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                ))}

}

function StatCard({
  label,
  value,
  color,
}: {
  label: string;
  value: number;
  color?: 'yellow' | 'red';
}) {
  const colorClass = color === 'yellow'
    ? 'border-yellow-200 bg-yellow-50'
    : color === 'red'
      ? 'border-red-200 bg-red-50'
      : 'border-gray-200 bg-white';

  const textColor = color === 'yellow'
    ? 'text-yellow-800'
    : color === 'red'
      ? 'text-red-800'
      : 'text-gray-900';

  return (
    <div className={`border rounded p-4 ${colorClass}`}>
      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">{label}</p>
      <p className={`text-2xl font-bold ${textColor}`}>{value}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function EditReservationPage() {
  const params = useParams();
  const router = useRouter();
  const id = params.id as string;

  const [reservation, setReservation] = useState<GuestReservationRow | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState(false);

  // 繝輔か繝ｼ繝 state
  const [checkInDate, setCheckInDate] = useState('');
  const [checkOutDate, setCheckOutDate] = useState('');
  const [adults, setAdults] = useState(1);
  const [children, setChildren] = useState(0);
  const [infants, setInfants] = useState(0);
  const [pets, setPets] = useState(0);
  const [cars, setCars] = useState(0);
  const [siteNumber, setSiteNumber] = useState('');
  const [specialRequests, setSpecialRequests] = useState('');
  const [paymentMethod, setPaymentMethod] = useState<PaymentMethod>('cash');
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState<PaymentStatus>('pending');
  const [totalAmount, setTotalAmount] = useState(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      const result = await fetchReservationByIdAdmin(id);
      if (result.error || !result.data) {
        setError(result.error ?? '莠育ｴ・′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ');
        setLoading(false);
        return;
      }
      const r = result.data;
      setReservation(r);
      setCheckInDate(r.check_in_date);
      setCheckOutDate(r.check_out_date);
      setAdults(r.adults ?? r.guests ?? 1);
      setChildren(r.children ?? 0);
      setInfants(r.infants ?? 0);
      setPets(r.pets ?? 0);
      setCars(r.cars ?? 0);
      setSiteNumber(r.site_number ?? '');
      setSpecialRequests(r.special_requests ?? '');
      setPaymentMethod(r.payment_method ?? 'cash');
      setPaymentStatus(r.payment_status ?? 'pending');
      setTotalAmount(Number(r.total_amount));
      setLoading(false);
    }
    load();
  }, [id]);

  const handleSubmit = useCallback(async () => {
    setError(null);
    setSuccess(false);
    setSaving(true);

    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    const adminEmail = user?.email ?? '荳肴・';

    const result = await updateReservation(
      id,
      {
        checkInDate,
        checkOutDate,
        guests: adults + children + infants,
        adults,
        children,
        infants,
        pets,
        cars,
        siteNumber,
        specialRequests,
        paymentMethod,
        paymentStatus,
        totalAmount,
      },
      adminEmail,
    );

    if (!result.success) {
      setError(result.error);
      setSaving(false);
      return;
    }

    setSuccess(true);
    setSaving(false);
    setTimeout(() => router.push(`/admin/reservations/${id}`), 1200);
  }, [id, checkInDate, checkOutDate, adults, children, infants, pets, cars, siteNumber, specialRequests, paymentMethod, paymentStatus, totalAmount, router]);

  if (loading) {
    return <div className="max-w-3xl p-4 text-sm text-gray-400">隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳ｭ...</div>;
  }

  if (!reservation) {
    return (
      <div className="max-w-3xl">
        <Link href="/admin/reservations" className="text-sm text-blue-600 hover:underline mb-4 inline-block">
          &larr; 莠育ｴ・ｸ隕ｧ縺ｫ謌ｻ繧・
        </Link>

        </div>
      </div>
    );

          莠育ｴ・ｷｨ髮・ {generateReceptionCode(r.id)}
        </h1>

interface OptionEntry {
  name?: string;
  quantity?: number;
  subtotal?: number;
  [key: string]: Json | undefined;
}

function parseOptions(json: Json): OptionEntry[] {
  if (Array.isArray(json)) {
    return json as OptionEntry[];
  }
  return [];
}

function Section({ title, children }: { title: string; children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <section className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-5 mb-4">
      <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-3 border-b border-gray-100 pb-2">
        {title}
      </h2>
      {children}
    </section>
  );
}

      <dt className="w-36 shrink-0 text-gray-500">{label}</dt>
      <dd className="text-gray-900">{value ?? '-'}</dd>

  );
}

    setLoading(true);
    const result = await fetchReservationByIdAdmin(id);
    if (result.error) {
      setError(result.error);
    } else if (!result.data) {
      setError('莠育ｴ・′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ');
    } else {
      setReservation(result.data);
    }
    const [notifs, logs] = await Promise.all([
      fetchNotificationsByReservation(id),
      fetchActionsByTarget('reservation', id),
    ]);
    setNotifications(notifs);
    setActionLogs(logs);
    setLoading(false);
  }, [id]);

    setCancelling(true);

    if (result.success) {
      setCancelConfirm(false);
      await loadData();
    } else {
      setError(result.error ?? '繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆');

        </div>
      </div>
    );

  const options = parseOptions(r.options_json);

    <div className="max-w-3xl">
      {/* 繝倥ャ繝 */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <Link
            href="/admin/reservations"
            className="text-sm text-blue-600 hover:underline"
          >
            &larr; 荳隕ｧ
          </Link>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">

            className={`inline-block rounded-full px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium ${badge.className}`}
          >
            {badge.label}
          </span>
        </div>

          {r.status !== 'cancelled' && (

              <Link
                href={`/admin/reservations/${r.id}/edit`}
                className="px-3 py-1.5 text-sm text-gray-700 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-50"
              >
                邱ｨ髮・
              </Link>
              {cancelConfirm ? (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <button
                    onClick={handleCancel}
                    disabled={cancelling}
                    className="px-3 py-1.5 text-sm text-white bg-red-600 rounded hover:bg-red-700 disabled:opacity-50"
                  >
                    {cancelling ? '蜃ｦ逅・ｸｭ...' : '繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ遒ｺ螳・}

import { useState } from 'react';

import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import {
  createAdminReservation,
  validateAdminReservation,
  type AdminReservationInput,
} from '@/lib/admin/createAdminReservation';
import { siteDetails } from '@/data/sitesDummyData';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type PaymentMethod = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_method'];
type PaymentStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_status'];

const PAYMENT_METHOD_OPTIONS: { value: PaymentMethod; label: string }[] = [
  { value: 'cash', label: '迴ｾ蝨ｰ謇輔＞' },
  { value: 'credit_card', label: '繧ｯ繝ｬ繧ｸ繝・ヨ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝・ },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: '驫陦梧険霎ｼ' },
];

const PAYMENT_STATUS_OPTIONS: { value: PaymentStatus; label: string }[] = [
  { value: 'pending', label: '豎ｺ貂亥ｾ・■' },
  { value: 'paid', label: '豎ｺ貂域ｸ医∩' },
];

function getDefaultPaymentStatus(method: PaymentMethod): PaymentStatus {
  return method === 'cash' ? 'pending' : 'pending';
}

function Label({ children, required }: { children: React.ReactNode; required?: boolean }) {
  return (
    <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
      {children}
      {required && <span className="text-red-500 ml-0.5">*</span>}
    </label>
  );
}

export default function AdminReservationNewPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const [form, setForm] = useState<AdminReservationInput>({
    userName: '',
    userPhone: '',
    userEmail: '',
    checkInDate: '',
    checkOutDate: '',
    guests: 1,
    siteNumber: '',
    paymentMethod: 'cash',
    paymentStatus: 'pending',
    totalAmount: 0,
    specialRequests: '',
  });

  const update = <K extends keyof AdminReservationInput>(
    key: K,
    value: AdminReservationInput[K],
  ) => {
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }));
    setError(null);
  };

  const nights =
    form.checkInDate && form.checkOutDate && form.checkOutDate > form.checkInDate
      ? Math.ceil(
          (new Date(form.checkOutDate).getTime() - new Date(form.checkInDate).getTime()) /
            (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24),
        )
      : 0;

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError(null);

    const validationError = validateAdminReservation(form);
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError);
      return;
    }

    setSaving(true);
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    const result = await createAdminReservation({ ...form, adminEmail: user?.email ?? undefined });
    setSaving(false);

    if (!result.success) {
      setError(result.error);
      return;
    }

    router.push(`/admin/reservations/${result.reservation.id}`);
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-2xl">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-6">謇句虚莠育ｴ・匳骭ｲ</h1>

      {error && (
        <div className="mb-4 rounded border border-red-200 bg-red-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-red-700 whitespace-pre-wrap">
          {error}
        </div>
      )}

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-6">
        {/* --- 繧ｲ繧ｹ繝域ュ蝣ｱ --- */}
        <section className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded p-5">
          <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-4 border-b border-gray-100 pb-2">
            繧ｲ繧ｹ繝域ュ蝣ｱ
          </h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div>
              <Label required>莠育ｴ・・錐</Label>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={form.userName}
                onChange={(e) => update('userName', e.target.value)}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500"
                placeholder="螻ｱ逕ｰ 螟ｪ驛・
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <Label>髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ</Label>
              <input
                type="tel"
                value={form.userPhone}
                onChange={(e) => update('userPhone', e.target.value)}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500"
                placeholder="090-1234-5678"
              />

  cancelled: { label: '繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ', className: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800' },

  pending: { className: 'bg-yellow-50 text-yellow-700' },
  paid: { className: 'bg-green-50 text-green-700' },
  refunded: { className: 'bg-gray-50 text-gray-600' },
  failed: { className: 'bg-red-50 text-red-700' },

  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState<ReservationStatus | 'all'>('all');
  const [dateFilter, setDateFilter] = useState('');

  const loadReservations = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);

    const filter: ReservationListFilter = {};
    if (statusFilter !== 'all') filter.status = statusFilter;
    if (dateFilter) filter.checkInDate = dateFilter;

    const result = await fetchReservations(filter);
    if (result.error) {
      setError(result.error);
    } else {
      setReservations(result.data);
    }
    setLoading(false);
  }, [statusFilter, dateFilter]);

  useEffect(() => {
    loadReservations();
  }, [loadReservations]);

  return (
    <div className="max-w-6xl">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-4">莠育ｴ・ｸ隕ｧ</h1>

            onChange={(e) => setDateFilter(e.target.value)}
            className="border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-1.5 text-sm bg-white"
          />
        </div>
        {dateFilter && (
          <button
            onClick={() => setDateFilter('')}

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import Stripe from 'stripe';

const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY!, {
  apiVersion: '2024-12-18.acacia',
});

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { amount } = await request.json();

    const paymentIntent = await stripe.paymentIntents.create({
      amount: amount,
      currency: 'jpy',
      automatic_payment_methods: {
        enabled: true,
      },
    });

    return NextResponse.json({ clientSecret: paymentIntent.client_secret });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error creating payment intent:', error);
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: 'Payment intent creation failed' },
      { status: 500 }
    );
  }
}
=== FILE: C:\Users\takam\Downloads\キャンプ場システム開発\VScode\campsite-booking\src\app\api\import-reservations\route.ts ===
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import { generateQrToken } from '@/lib/generateQrToken';
import {
  validateReservation,
  formatAdminErrors,
  calculateNights,
} from '@/lib/validateReservation';
import type {
  ImportParsedRow,
  ImportRowError,
  ImportDuplicate,
  ImportExecutionResult,
} from '@/types/import';
import type { Json } from '@/types/database';
import { logAdminAction } from '@/lib/admin/actionLog';

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json();
    const rows: ImportParsedRow[] = body.rows;
    const errorRows: ImportRowError[] = body.errorRows ?? [];
    const duplicateRows: ImportDuplicate[] = body.duplicateRows ?? [];
    const fileName: string = body.fileName ?? '';
    const executedBy: string = body.executedBy ?? '';

    if (!Array.isArray(rows) || rows.length === 0) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: '蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ蟇ｾ雎｡縺ｮ陦後′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ' },
        { status: 400 },
      );
    }

    // 荳企剞繝√ぉ繝・け・井ｸ蠎ｦ縺ｫ100莉ｶ縺ｾ縺ｧ・・
    if (rows.length > 100) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: '荳蠎ｦ縺ｫ蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ繧√ｋ縺ｮ縺ｯ100莉ｶ縺ｾ縺ｧ縺ｧ縺・ },
        { status: 400 },
      );
    }

    const totalRows = rows.length + errorRows.length + duplicateRows.length;

    // import_job 繧剃ｽ懈・
    const { data: jobData, error: jobError } = await supabase
      .from('import_jobs')
      .insert({
        executed_by: executedBy,
        file_name: fileName,
        total_rows: totalRows,
        success_count: 0,
        error_count: errorRows.length + duplicateRows.length,
      })
      .select('id')
      .single();

    if (jobError || !jobData) {
      console.error('[import-reservations] Failed to create import_job:', jobError);
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: '蜿冶ｾｼ繧ｸ繝ｧ繝悶・菴懈・縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆' },
        { status: 500 },
      );
    }

    const jobId = jobData.id;

    const result: ImportExecutionResult = {
      jobId,
      insertedCount: 0,
      failedCount: 0,
      failures: [],
    };

    // 繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ陦後ｒ險倬鹸
    if (errorRows.length > 0) {
      await supabase.from('import_job_rows').insert(
        errorRows.map((row) => ({
          import_job_id: jobId,
          row_number: row.rowIndex,
          raw_data_json: row.raw as unknown as Json,
          status: 'error',
          error_message: row.errors.join(' / '),
        })),
      );
    }

    // 驥崎､・｡後ｒ險倬鹸
    if (duplicateRows.length > 0) {
      await supabase.from('import_job_rows').insert(
        duplicateRows.map((dup) => ({
          import_job_id: jobId,
          row_number: dup.rowIndex,
          raw_data_json: dup.parsed as unknown as Json,
          status: 'error',
          error_message: `譌｢蟄倅ｺ育ｴ・→驥崎､・ ${dup.existingCheckIn} 縲・${dup.existingCheckOut}`,
        })),
      );
    }

    // 1莉ｶ縺壹▽ INSERT・亥・騾壹ヰ繝ｪ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ + 驥崎､・メ繧ｧ繝・け蜷ｫ繧・・
    for (const row of rows) {
      // 蜈ｱ騾壹ヰ繝ｪ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・磯㍾隍・メ繧ｧ繝・け蜷ｫ繧・・
      const validation = await validateReservation({
        siteNumber: row.siteNumber,
        checkInDate: row.checkInDate,
        checkOutDate: row.checkOutDate,
        guests: row.guests,
        source: 'import',
      });

      if (!validation.valid) {
        const errorMsg = formatAdminErrors(validation.errors);
        result.failedCount++;
        result.failures.push({
          rowIndex: row.rowIndex,
          error: errorMsg,
        });
        await supabase.from('import_job_rows').insert({
          import_job_id: jobId,
          row_number: row.rowIndex,
          raw_data_json: row as unknown as Json,
          status: 'error',
          error_message: errorMsg,
        });
        continue;
      }

      // 螳ｿ豕頑焚險育ｮ暦ｼ亥・騾壹Θ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｪ繝・ぅ・・
      const nights = calculateNights(row.checkInDate, row.checkOutDate);

      const { data: insertData, error: insertError } = await supabase
        .from('guest_reservations')
        .insert({
          user_name: row.userName,
          user_phone: row.userPhone || null,
          user_email: row.userEmail || null,
          check_in_date: row.checkInDate,
          check_out_date: row.checkOutDate,
          nights,
          guests: row.guests,
          site_number: row.siteNumber,
          total_amount: 0, // 繧､繝ｳ繝昴・繝域凾縺ｯ驥鷹｡肴悴險ｭ螳・
          status: 'confirmed' as const,
          payment_method: row.paymentMethod,
          payment_status: 'pending' as const,
          qr_token: generateQrToken(),
          options_json: [],
          agreed_cancellation: true,
          agreed_terms: true,
          agreed_sns: false,
          special_requests: row.specialRequests || null,
        })
        .select('id')
        .single();

      if (insertError) {
        result.failedCount++;
        result.failures.push({
          rowIndex: row.rowIndex,
          error: insertError.message,
        });
        await supabase.from('import_job_rows').insert({
          import_job_id: jobId,
          row_number: row.rowIndex,
          raw_data_json: row as unknown as Json,
          status: 'error',
          error_message: insertError.message,
        });
      } else {
        result.insertedCount++;
        await supabase.from('import_job_rows').insert({
          import_job_id: jobId,
          row_number: row.rowIndex,
          raw_data_json: row as unknown as Json,
          status: 'success',
          created_reservation_id: insertData?.id ?? null,
        });
      }
    }

    // import_job 縺ｮ繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝医ｒ譖ｴ譁ｰ
    await supabase
      .from('import_jobs')
      .update({
        success_count: result.insertedCount,
        error_count: errorRows.length + duplicateRows.length + result.failedCount,
      })
      .eq('id', jobId);

    // 謫堺ｽ懊Ο繧ｰ
    await logAdminAction({
      adminEmail: executedBy,
      actionType: 'import_execute',
      targetType: 'import_job',
      targetId: jobId,
      after: {
        file_name: fileName,
        total_rows: totalRows,
        success_count: result.insertedCount,
        error_count: errorRows.length + duplicateRows.length + result.failedCount,
      },
    });

    return NextResponse.json(result);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[import-reservations] Error:', err);
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: '蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ蜃ｦ逅・ｸｭ縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺ｾ縺励◆' },
      { status: 500 },
    );
  }
}

// ============================================================
// 繝ｦ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｪ繝・ぅ

function formatDate(dateStr: string): string {
  const d = new Date(dateStr);
  const weekdays = ["譌･", "譛・, "轣ｫ", "豌ｴ", "譛ｨ", "驥・, "蝨・];
  return `${d.getFullYear()}蟷ｴ${d.getMonth() + 1}譛・{d.getDate()}譌･・・{weekdays[d.getDay()]}・荏;
}

function formatPrice(price: number): string {
  return price.toLocaleString("ja-JP");
}

function getPaymentLabel(method: "credit_card" | "on_site" | null): string {
  if (method === "credit_card") return "繧ｯ繝ｬ繧ｸ繝・ヨ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝会ｼ井ｺ句燕豎ｺ貂茨ｼ・;
  if (method === "on_site") return "迴ｾ蝨ｰ豎ｺ貂・;
  return "譛ｪ驕ｸ謚・;
}

// ============================================================
// 繧ｵ繝悶さ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・
// ============================================================

function SectionHeading({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <h2 className="text-[15px] font-bold text-gray-800 pb-2 mb-4 border-b-2 border-emerald-600">
      {children}
    </h2>
  );
}

function SummaryRow({
  label,
  value,
  bold,
}: {
  label: string;
  value: React.ReactNode;
  bold?: boolean;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
      <span className={bold ? "font-bold text-gray-900" : "text-gray-500"}>
        {label}
      </span>
      <span className={bold ? "text-xl font-bold text-emerald-700" : "font-medium text-gray-800"}>
        {value}
      </span>
    </div>
  );
}

function CheckBadge({ checked, label }: { checked: boolean; label: string }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
      <span
        className={`flex-shrink-0 w-5 h-5 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center ${
          checked ? "bg-emerald-500" : "bg-gray-300"
        }`}
      >
        {checked ? (
          <svg className="w-3 h-3 text-white" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth={3}>
            <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" />
          </svg>
        ) : (
          <svg className="w-3 h-3 text-white" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth={3}>
            <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12" />
          </svg>
        )}
      </span>
      <span className={`text-sm ${checked ? "text-gray-700" : "text-gray-400"}`}>
        {label}
      </span>
    </div>
  );
}

  const plan = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.plan);
  const site = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.site);
  const options = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.options);
  const policy = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.policy);

  const resetDraft = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.reset);

              value={`ﾂ･${formatPrice(site.sitePrice)}`}
            />
            {site.designationFee > 0 && (
              <SummaryRow

                value={`ﾂ･${formatPrice(site.designationFee)}`}

                    <span className="text-gray-600">
                      繝ｻ{opt?.name ?? "荳肴・縺ｪ繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ"}
                      {r.quantity > 1 && ` ﾃ・{r.quantity}`}
                      {r.days && r.days > 1 && ` (${r.days}譌･髢・`}
                    </span>
                    <span className="font-medium">ﾂ･{formatPrice(r.subtotal)}</span>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
              {options.events.map((e) => {
                const opt = optionMap.get(e.optionId);
                return (
                  <div key={e.optionId} className="flex justify-between">
                    <span className="text-gray-600">
                      繝ｻ{opt?.name ?? "荳肴・縺ｪ繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ"}
                      {e.people > 1 && ` ﾃ・{e.people}蜷港}
                    </span>
                    <span className="font-medium">ﾂ･{formatPrice(e.subtotal)}</span>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
              <div className="flex justify-between pt-2 border-t border-gray-100">
                <span className="text-gray-500">繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ蜷郁ｨ・/span>
                <span className="font-medium">ﾂ･{formatPrice(optionsTotal)}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </section>

        {/* ============================================ */}
        {/* 隕冗ｴ・酔諢冗憾諷・*/}
        {/* ============================================ */}
        <section className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-gray-200 p-5 sm:p-6 mb-6">
          <SectionHeading>隕冗ｴ・・蜷梧э莠矩・/SectionHeading>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <CheckBadge checked={policy.agreedCancellation} label="繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ繝昴Μ繧ｷ繝ｼ縺ｫ蜷梧э貂医∩" />
