"use client";

import { useState, useCallback, useMemo, useEffect } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { OptionItem, OptionSelection, OptionsPayload, BookingContext, STORAGE_KEY_OPTIONS_PAYLOAD } from "@/types/options";
import { dummyOptions } from "@/data/optionsDummyData";
import { useBookingDraftStore } from "@/stores/bookingDraftStore";
import BookingSummaryBar from "@/components/booking/BookingSummaryBar";
import RentalOptionCard from "@/components/booking/RentalOptionCard";
import EventOptionCard from "@/components/booking/EventOptionCard";
import SelectedOptionsSummary from "@/components/booking/SelectedOptionsSummary";

// --- 蟆剰ｨ郁ｨ育ｮ励・繝ｫ繝代・ ---

function calcSubtotal(option: OptionItem, sel: OptionSelection): number {
  switch (option.priceType) {
    case "per_day":
      return option.price * sel.quantity * sel.days;
    case "per_person":
      return option.price * sel.people;
    case "per_unit":
      return option.price * sel.quantity;
    case "fixed":
      return sel.quantity > 0 ? option.price : 0;
    default:
      return 0;
  }
}

// --- 繝・ヵ繧ｩ繝ｫ繝医・ selection 繧堤函謌・---

function defaultSelection(optionId: string, nights: number): OptionSelection {
  return { optionId, quantity: 0, days: nights, people: 0, subtotal: 0 };
}

export default function OptionsPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const stay = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.stay);
  const site = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.site);
  const setOptions = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.setOptions);

  // 繧ｬ繝ｼ繝・ 螳ｿ豕頑律譛ｪ蜈･蜉・竊・TOP縲√し繧､繝域悴驕ｸ謚・竊・繧ｵ繧､繝磯∈謚・
  const hasStay = !!(stay.checkIn && stay.checkOut && stay.nights > 0);
  const hasSite = !!site.siteId;

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!hasStay) {
      router.replace("/");
    } else if (!hasSite) {
      router.replace("/booking/sites");
    }
  }, [hasStay, hasSite, router]);

  const booking: BookingContext = useMemo(
    () => ({
      checkInDate: stay.checkIn ?? "2026-05-02",
      checkOutDate: stay.checkOut ?? "2026-05-04",
      nights: stay.nights || 2,
      guests: stay.adults + stay.children || 4,
      siteId: site.siteId ?? "",
      siteNumber: site.siteNumber ?? "譛ｪ驕ｸ謚・,
      siteName: site.siteName ?? "譛ｪ驕ｸ謚・,
      sitePrice: site.sitePrice ?? 0,
      designationFee: site.designationFee ?? 0,
      areaName: site.areaName ?? "",
      subAreaName: site.subAreaName ?? "",
    }),
    [stay, site]
  );

  const options = dummyOptions.filter((o) => o.isActive);

  const rentalOptions = useMemo(
    () => options.filter((o) => o.category === "rental"),
    [options]
  );
  const eventOptions = useMemo(
    () => options.filter((o) => o.category === "event"),
    [options]
  );
  const optionMap = useMemo(
    () => new Map(options.map((o) => [o.id, o])),
    [options]
  );

  // --- 驕ｸ謚樒憾諷・---
  const [selections, setSelections] = useState<Map<string, OptionSelection>>(
    () => new Map()
  );

  /** selection 繧呈峩譁ｰ縺励※蟆剰ｨ医ｒ蜀崎ｨ育ｮ励☆繧九・繝ｫ繝代・ */
  const updateSelection = useCallback(
    (
      optionId: string,
      updater: (prev: OptionSelection) => Partial<OptionSelection>
    ) => {
      setSelections((prev) => {
        const next = new Map(prev);
        const current =
          next.get(optionId) ?? defaultSelection(optionId, booking.nights);
        const updated = { ...current, ...updater(current) };
        const opt = optionMap.get(optionId);
        updated.subtotal = opt ? calcSubtotal(opt, updated) : 0;
        next.set(optionId, updated);
        return next;
      });
    },
    [booking.nights, optionMap]
  );

  // --- 繧､繝吶Φ繝医ワ繝ｳ繝峨Λ ---

  const handleQuantityChange = useCallback(
    (optionId: string, quantity: number) => {
      updateSelection(optionId, (prev) => ({
        quantity,
        days: quantity === 0 ? booking.nights : prev.days,
      }));
    },
    [updateSelection, booking.nights]
  );

  const handleDaysChange = useCallback(
    (optionId: string, days: number) => {
      updateSelection(optionId, () => ({ days }));
    },
    [updateSelection]
  );

  const handlePeopleChange = useCallback(
    (optionId: string, people: number) => {
      updateSelection(optionId, () => ({ people }));
    },
    [updateSelection]
  );

  // --- 髮・ｨ・---

  const activeSelections = useMemo(
    () => Array.from(selections.values()).filter((s) => s.subtotal > 0),
    [selections]
  );

  const totalAmount = useMemo(
    () => activeSelections.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.subtotal, 0),
    [activeSelections]
  );

  // --- 遒ｺ隱咲判髱｢縺ｸ縺ｮ payload 逕滓・ ---

  const buildPayload = (): OptionsPayload => ({
    booking,
    selectedOptions: activeSelections,
    optionsTotalAmount: totalAmount,
  });

  const handleNext = () => {
    const payload = buildPayload();
    sessionStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY_OPTIONS_PAYLOAD, JSON.stringify(payload));

    // Zustand store 縺ｫ繧ゅが繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ驕ｸ謚槭ｒ菫晏ｭ假ｼ・onfirmation 繝壹・繧ｸ縺ｧ蜿ら・・・
    const rentals = activeSelections
      .filter((s) => optionMap.get(s.optionId)?.category === "rental")
      .map((s) => ({ optionId: s.optionId, quantity: s.quantity, days: s.days, subtotal: s.subtotal }));
    const events = activeSelections
      .filter((s) => optionMap.get(s.optionId)?.category === "event")
      .map((s) => ({ optionId: s.optionId, people: s.people, subtotal: s.subtotal }));
    setOptions({ rentals, events });

    router.push("/booking/terms-payment");
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-b from-emerald-50 via-white to-amber-50/30">
      <div className="max-w-lg mx-auto px-4 py-6 pb-56">
        {/* 繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ */}
        <div className="text-center mb-4">
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 tracking-wide mb-1">
            STEP 3 / 4
          </p>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800">
            繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ繝ｻ菴馴ｨ薙ｒ驕ｸ縺ｶ
          </h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
            蠢・ｦ√↑繧ゅ・縺縺題ｿｽ蜉縺ｧ縺阪∪縺吶ゅせ繧ｭ繝・・繧０K・・
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* 莠育ｴ・し繝槭Μ繝ｼ */}
        <BookingSummaryBar booking={booking} />

        {/* 繝ｬ繝ｳ繧ｿ繝ｫ / 繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ */}
        <section className="mb-8">
          <div className="mb-3">
            <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-gray-800">
              繝ｬ繝ｳ繧ｿ繝ｫ / 繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ
            </h2>
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {rentalOptions.map((opt) => (
              <RentalOptionCard
                key={opt.id}
                option={opt}
                selection={selections.get(opt.id)}
                nights={booking.nights}
                onChangeQuantity={handleQuantityChange}
                onChangeDays={handleDaysChange}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* 繧､繝吶Φ繝・/ 菴馴ｨ・*/}
        <section className="mb-8">
          <div className="mb-3">
            <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-gray-800">
              繧､繝吶Φ繝・/ 菴馴ｨ・
            </h2>
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {eventOptions.map((opt) => (
              <EventOptionCard
                key={opt.id}
                option={opt}
                selection={selections.get(opt.id)}
                onChangePeople={handlePeopleChange}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>

      {/* ===== 繝輔ャ繧ｿ繝ｼ蝗ｺ螳壹お繝ｪ繧｢ ===== */}
      <div className="fixed bottom-0 inset-x-0 bg-white/95 backdrop-blur border-t border-gray-200 shadow-[0_-4px_24px_rgba(0,0,0,0.06)]">
        <div className="max-w-lg mx-auto px-4 py-3">
          {/* 驕ｸ謚槫・螳ｹ縺ｾ縺ｨ繧・*/}
          {activeSelections.length > 0 && (
            <div className="mb-3 max-h-36 overflow-y-auto">
              <SelectedOptionsSummary
                selections={activeSelections}
                options={options}
                totalAmount={totalAmount}
              />
            </div>
          )}

          {activeSelections.length === 0 && (
            <p className="text-center text-sm text-gray-400 mb-3">
              繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ縺ｪ縺励〒繧よｬ｡縺ｸ騾ｲ繧√∪縺・
            </p>
          )}

          {/* 繝翫ン繧ｲ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繝懊ち繝ｳ */}
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Link
              href="/booking/sites"
              className="flex-1 text-center py-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-300 text-gray-600 font-medium hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors text-sm"
            >
              竊・蜑阪∈
            </Link>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={handleNext}
              className="flex-[2] py-3 rounded-xl bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-700 text-white font-semibold transition-colors text-sm shadow-sm"
            >
              谺｡縺ｸ 竊・遒ｺ隱咲判髱｢
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function formatDate(dateStr: string): string {
  const d = new Date(dateStr);
  const weekdays = ["譌･", "譛・, "轣ｫ", "豌ｴ", "譛ｨ", "驥・, "蝨・];
  return `${d.getFullYear()}蟷ｴ${d.getMonth() + 1}譛・{d.getDate()}譌･・・{weekdays[d.getDay()]}・荏;
}

/** 驥鷹｡阪ｒ繧ｫ繝ｳ繝槫玄蛻・ｊ縺ｧ陦ｨ遉ｺ */
function formatPrice(price: number): string {
  return price.toLocaleString("ja-JP");
}

// ============================================================
// 繧ｵ繝悶さ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・ 繧ｻ繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ隕句・縺・
// ============================================================

function SectionHeading({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <h2 className="text-[15px] font-bold text-gray-800 pb-2 mb-4 border-b-2 border-emerald-600">
      {children}
    </h2>
  );
}

// ============================================================
// 繧ｵ繝悶さ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・ 繧｢繧ｳ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繧ｪ繝ｳ繧ｻ繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ
// ============================================================

function AccordionSection({
  title,
  defaultOpen = false,
  children,
}: {
  title: string;
  defaultOpen?: boolean;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);

  return (
    <div className="border border-gray-200 rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        className="w-full flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3.5 bg-stone-50 hover:bg-stone-100 transition-colors text-left"
      >
        <span className="font-semibold text-gray-700 text-sm">
          {title}
        </span>
        <svg
          className={`w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 transition-transform duration-200 ${isOpen ? "rotate-180" : ""}`}
          fill="none"
          viewBox="0 0 24 24"
          stroke="currentColor"
          strokeWidth={2}
        >
          <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" d="M19 9l-7 7-7-7" />
        </svg>
      </button>
      {isOpen && (
        <div className="px-4 py-4 bg-white text-sm text-gray-600 leading-relaxed border-t border-gray-100">
          {children}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============================================================
// 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繝壹・繧ｸ繧ｳ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・
// ============================================================

export default function TermsPaymentPage() {
  const router = useRouter();

  // --- store 縺九ｉ蠕ｩ蜈・畑縺ｫ隱ｭ縺ｿ蜿悶ｊ ---
  const storeStay = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.stay);
  const storeSite = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.site);
  const storePolicy = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.policy);
  const storePayment = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.payment);
  const setStorePolicy = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.setPolicy);
  const setStorePayment = useBookingDraftStore((s) => s.setPayment);

  // 繧ｬ繝ｼ繝・ 螳ｿ豕頑律繝ｻ繧ｵ繧､繝域悴驕ｸ謚槭↑繧牙燕縺ｮ繝壹・繧ｸ縺ｸ
  const hasStay = !!(storeStay.checkIn && storeStay.checkOut && storeStay.nights > 0);
  const hasSite = !!storeSite.siteId;

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!hasStay) {
      router.replace("/");
    } else if (!hasSite) {
      router.replace("/booking/sites");
    }
  }, [hasStay, hasSite, router]);

  // --- sessionStorage 縺九ｉ繝壹う繝ｭ繝ｼ繝芽ｪｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ ---
  const [payload, setPayload] = useState<OptionsPayload | null>(null);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      const stored = sessionStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY_OPTIONS_PAYLOAD);
      if (stored) {
        setPayload(JSON.parse(stored) as OptionsPayload);
      }
    } catch {
      // 荳肴ｭ｣繝・・繧ｿ 窶・payload 縺ｯ null 縺ｮ縺ｾ縺ｾ
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  // --- 繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ蜷阪・騾・ｼ輔″繝槭ャ繝・---
  const optionMap = useMemo(
    () => new Map(dummyOptions.map((o) => [o.id, o])),
    []
  );

  // --- 迥ｶ諷狗ｮ｡逅・ｼ・tore 縺九ｉ蛻晄悄蛟､繧貞ｾｩ蜈・ｼ・---
  const [agreedCancelPolicy, setAgreedCancelPolicy] = useState(storePolicy.agreedCancellation);
  const [agreedTerms, setAgreedTerms] = useState(storePolicy.agreedTerms);
  const [agreedSns, setAgreedSns] = useState(storePolicy.agreedSns);
  const [selectedPayment, setSelectedPayment] = useState<string | null>(storePayment.method);

  const canProceed = agreedCancelPolicy && agreedTerms && selectedPayment !== null;

  // --- 遒ｺ隱咲判髱｢縺ｸ騾ｲ繧繝上Φ繝峨Λ ---
  const handleProceed = () => {
    if (!payload || !canProceed) return;

    // store 縺ｫ菫晏ｭ・
    setStorePolicy({
      agreedCancellation: agreedCancelPolicy,
      agreedTerms,
      agreedSns,
    });
    setStorePayment({
      method: selectedPayment as "credit_card" | "on_site",
    });

    router.push("/booking/confirmation");
  };

  // --- 繝ｭ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｳ繧ｰ迥ｶ諷・---
  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-b from-stone-50 to-emerald-50/30 flex items-center justify-center">
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳ｭ...</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // --- 繝・・繧ｿ縺ｪ縺励ヵ繧ｩ繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ ---
  if (!payload) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-b from-stone-50 to-emerald-50/30 flex items-center justify-center px-4">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-gray-200 p-8 max-w-sm w-full text-center">
          <p className="text-gray-700 font-semibold mb-2">莠育ｴ・ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ縺瑚ｦ九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-6">繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ驕ｸ謚樒判髱｢縺九ｉ繧・ｊ逶ｴ縺励※縺上□縺輔＞縲・/p>
          <Link
            href="/booking/options"
            className="inline-block px-6 py-2.5 rounded-xl bg-emerald-600 text-white text-sm font-semibold hover:bg-emerald-700 transition-colors"
          >
            繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ驕ｸ謚槭↓謌ｻ繧・
          </Link>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const { booking, selectedOptions, optionsTotalAmount } = payload;
  const totalAmount = booking.sitePrice + booking.designationFee + optionsTotalAmount;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-b from-stone-50 to-emerald-50/30 py-8 pb-28">
      <div className="container mx-auto px-4 max-w-2xl">
        {/* ============================================ */}
        {/* A. 繝壹・繧ｸ繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ */}
        {/* ============================================ */}
        <div className="text-center mb-10">
          <Link
            href="/booking/options"
            className="inline-block text-emerald-700 hover:text-emerald-800 text-sm transition-colors"
          >
            竊・繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ驕ｸ謚槭↓謌ｻ繧・
          </Link>
          <h1 className="text-2xl sm:text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900 mt-4 tracking-tight">
            隕冗ｴ・・謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-500 mt-2 text-sm sm:text-base max-w-md mx-auto">
            蜀・ｮｹ繧偵＃遒ｺ隱阪・縺・∴縲∝茜逕ｨ隕冗ｴ・∈縺ｮ蜷梧э縺ｨ縺頑髪謇輔＞譁ｹ豕輔・驕ｸ謚槭ｒ縺企｡倥＞縺励∪縺吶・
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* ============================================ */}
        {/* B. 莠育ｴ・・螳ｹ繧ｵ繝槭Μ繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝・*/}
        {/* ============================================ */}
        <section className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-gray-200 p-5 sm:p-6 mb-6">
          <SectionHeading>莠育ｴ・・螳ｹ縺ｮ遒ｺ隱・/SectionHeading>

          <div className="space-y-2.5 text-sm text-gray-700">
            <div className="flex justify-between">
              <span className="text-gray-500">蛻ｩ逕ｨ譌･</span>
              <span className="font-medium">{formatDate(booking.checkInDate)}</span>
            </div>
            <div className="flex justify-between">
              <span className="text-gray-500">螳ｿ豕頑焚</span>
              <span className="font-medium">{booking.nights}豕顎booking.nights + 1}譌･</span>
            </div>
            <div className="flex justify-between">
              <span className="text-gray-500">莠ｺ謨ｰ</span>

            <div className="flex justify-between">

            </div>

            {/* 驕ｸ謚槭が繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ */}

                {selectedOptions.map((sel) => {
                  const opt = optionMap.get(sel.optionId);
                  return (
                    <div key={sel.optionId} className="flex justify-between mt-1.5">
                      <span className="text-gray-600">繝ｻ{opt?.name ?? "荳肴・縺ｪ繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ"}</span>

            {selectedOptions.length === 0 && (
              <div className="border-t border-gray-100 pt-3 mt-3">
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ縺ｮ驕ｸ謚槭↑縺・/p>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* 驥鷹｡肴・邏ｰ */}

'use client';

import { Suspense, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useSearchParams } from 'next/navigation';
import QRCodeDisplay from '@/components/QRCodeDisplay';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';

export default function CheckInPage() {
  return (
    <Suspense fallback={<div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center">隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳ｭ...</div>}>
      <CheckInContent />
    </Suspense>
  );
}

function CheckInContent() {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const reservationId = searchParams.get('id');
  const [reservation, setReservation] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (reservationId) {
      fetchReservation();
    }
  }, [reservationId]);

  const fetchReservation = async () => {
    if (!reservationId) return;
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('reservations')
      .select('*')
      .eq('id', reservationId)
      .single();

    if (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching reservation:', error);
    } else {
      setReservation(data);
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  if (loading) return <div>隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳ｭ...</div>;
  if (!reservation) return <div>莠育ｴ・′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ</div>;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6 max-w-md w-full text-center">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ</h1>
        <p className="mb-4">縺薙・QR繧ｳ繝ｼ繝峨ｒ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ遶ｯ譛ｫ縺ｫ縺九＊縺励※縺上□縺輔＞</p>
        <QRCodeDisplay value={reservationId!} size={200} />
        <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-600">
          <p>莠育ｴИD: {reservationId}</p>
          <p>繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･: {new Date(reservation.check_in_date).toLocaleDateString('ja-JP')}</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/** ISO 譌･莉俶枚蟄怜・ (yyyy-mm-dd) 竊・陦ｨ遉ｺ逕ｨ (yyyy/mm/dd) */
function formatDate(iso: string): string {
  return iso.replace(/-/g, "/");
}

/** 2 縺､縺ｮ ISO 譌･莉倬俣縺ｮ豕頑焚繧定ｨ育ｮ・*/
function calcNights(checkIn: string, checkOut: string): number {
  const diff =
    new Date(checkOut).getTime() - new Date(checkIn).getTime();
  return Math.max(0, Math.round(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)));
}

/** 莉頑律縺ｮ譌･莉倥ｒ yyyy-mm-dd 縺ｧ霑斐☆ */
function todayISO(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, "0")}`;
}

export default function Home() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { stay, setStay } = useBookingDraftStore();

  const today = useMemo(() => todayISO(), []);

  const nights = useMemo(() => {
    if (!stay.checkIn || !stay.checkOut) return 0;
    return calcNights(stay.checkIn, stay.checkOut);
  }, [stay.checkIn, stay.checkOut]);

  const handleCheckInChange = useCallback(
    (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
      const newCheckIn = e.target.value;
      const updates: { checkIn: string; checkOut?: string; nights?: number } = {
        checkIn: newCheckIn,
      };
      if (stay.checkOut && newCheckIn >= stay.checkOut) {
        updates.checkOut = "";
        updates.nights = 0;
      } else if (stay.checkOut) {
        updates.nights = calcNights(newCheckIn, stay.checkOut);
      }
      setStay(updates);
    },
    [stay.checkOut, setStay],
  );

  const handleCheckOutChange = useCallback(
    (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
      const newCheckOut = e.target.value;
      const n = stay.checkIn ? calcNights(stay.checkIn, newCheckOut) : 0;
      setStay({ checkOut: newCheckOut, nights: n });
    },
    [stay.checkIn, setStay],
  );

  const canProceed = !!(stay.checkIn && stay.checkOut && nights > 0);

  const handleProceed = () => {
    if (!canProceed) return;
    setStay({ nights });
    router.push("/booking/plans");
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-white">
      <div className="max-w-md mx-auto px-4 py-6 md:max-w-2xl">

        {/* ===== 繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ ===== */}
        <header className="mb-8">
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800">
            繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ莠育ｴ・          </h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-2">
            譌･莉倥ｒ驕ｸ繧薙〒繧ｵ繧､繝医ｒ莠育ｴ・＠縺ｾ縺励ｇ縺・          </p>
        </header>

        {/* ===== 譌･莉伜・蜉帙お繝ｪ繧｢ ===== */}
        <section className="border border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-4 mb-6">
          <h2 className="text-base font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-3">
            螳ｿ豕頑律繧帝∈謚・          </h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 mb-3">
            {/* 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ */}
            <div>
              <label htmlFor="checkIn" className="block text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ</label>
              <input
                id="checkIn"
                type="date"
                min={today}
                value={stay.checkIn ?? ""}
                onChange={handleCheckInChange}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-700 bg-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-400"
              />
            </div>
            {/* 繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝・*/}
            <div>
              <label htmlFor="checkOut" className="block text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝・/label>
              <input
                id="checkOut"
                type="date"
                min={stay.checkIn || today}
                value={stay.checkOut ?? ""}
                onChange={handleCheckOutChange}
                disabled={!stay.checkIn}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-700 bg-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-400 disabled:bg-gray-100 disabled:text-gray-400"
              />
            </div>
          </div>
          {/* 豕頑焚陦ｨ遉ｺ */}
          <div className="text-sm text-gray-600 bg-gray-50 rounded px-3 py-2 text-center">
            {nights > 0 ? (
              <span className="font-medium">
                {stay.checkIn && formatDate(stay.checkIn)} 縲・{stay.checkOut && formatDate(stay.checkOut)}・・strong>{nights}豕・/strong>・・              </span>
            ) : (
              <span className="text-gray-400">譌･莉倥ｒ驕ｸ謚槭＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞</span>
            )}
          </div>

        <section className="mb-6">

            髢句ぎ莠亥ｮ壹・繧､繝吶Φ繝・          </h2>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mb-3">
            窶ｻ 繧､繝吶Φ繝亥盾蜉縺ｮ縺泌ｸ梧悍縺ｯ縲∽ｺ育ｴ・凾縺ｮ繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ驕ｸ謚樒判髱｢縺ｧ縺企∈縺ｳ縺・◆縺縺代∪縺吶・          </p>
          <div className="flex gap-3 overflow-x-auto pb-2 -mx-4 px-4">

                key={event.title}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useParams, useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import type { ReservationDetail } from '@/types/reservation';
import { fetchReservationById } from '@/lib/fetchReservationById';
import QrDisplayCard from '@/components/reservation/QrDisplayCard';
import ReservationSummaryCard from '@/components/reservation/ReservationSummaryCard';
import NoticeSection from '@/components/reservation/NoticeSection';
import ReservationStatusBadge from '@/components/reservation/ReservationStatusBadge';

type PageState =
  | { type: 'loading' }
  | { type: 'error'; message: string }
  | { type: 'not-found' }
  | { type: 'loaded'; reservation: ReservationDetail };

export default function ReservationQrPage() {
  const params = useParams();
  const router = useRouter();
  const reservationId = params.id as string;

  const [state, setState] = useState<PageState>({ type: 'loading' });

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;

    async function load() {
      try {
        const data = await fetchReservationById(reservationId);
        if (cancelled) return;

        if (!data) {
          setState({ type: 'not-found' });
        } else {
          setState({ type: 'loaded', reservation: data });
        }
      } catch {
        if (cancelled) return;
        setState({
          type: 'error',
          message: '莠育ｴ・ュ蝣ｱ縺ｮ蜿門ｾ励↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆',
        });
      }
    }

    load();
    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
    };
  }, [reservationId]);

  // ---- 繝ｭ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｳ繧ｰ ----
  if (state.type === 'loading') {
    return (
      <div className="mx-auto min-h-screen max-w-md bg-gray-50 px-4 py-8">
        <div className="animate-pulse space-y-6">
          {/* 繧ｿ繧､繝医Ν鬪ｨ譬ｼ */}
          <div className="space-y-2 text-center">
            <div className="mx-auto h-6 w-48 rounded bg-gray-200" />
            <div className="mx-auto h-4 w-64 rounded bg-gray-200" />
          </div>
          {/* QR繧ｳ繝ｼ繝蛾ｪｨ譬ｼ */}
          <div className="flex justify-center">
            <div className="h-[260px] w-[260px] rounded-2xl bg-gray-200" />
          </div>
          {/* 繧ｫ繝ｼ繝蛾ｪｨ譬ｼ */}
          <div className="h-64 rounded-xl bg-gray-200" />
          <div className="h-48 rounded-xl bg-gray-200" />
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // ---- 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ ----
  if (state.type === 'error') {
    return (
      <div className="mx-auto flex min-h-screen max-w-md flex-col items-center justify-center bg-gray-50 px-4 py-8">
        <div className="w-full rounded-xl border border-red-200 bg-white p-8 text-center shadow-sm">
          <div className="mx-auto mb-4 flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-red-100">

            </svg>
          </div>

            譎る俣繧偵♀縺・※蜀榊ｺｦ縺願ｩｦ縺励￥縺縺輔＞
          </p>

              onClick={() => window.location.reload()}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { usePathname, useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';

const menuItems = [
  { href: '/admin', label: '繝繝・す繝･繝懊・繝・ },
  { href: '/admin/reservations', label: '莠育ｴ・ｸ隕ｧ' },
  { href: '/admin/reservations/new', label: '謇句虚莠育ｴ・匳骭ｲ' },
  { href: '/admin/plans', label: '繝励Λ繝ｳ邂｡逅・ },
  { href: '/admin/sites', label: '繧ｵ繧､繝育ｮ｡逅・ },
  { href: '/admin/rules', label: '雋ｩ螢ｲ繝ｫ繝ｼ繝ｫ' },
  { href: '/admin/import', label: '蜿冶ｾｼ邂｡逅・ },
  { href: '/admin/notifications', label: '騾夂衍繝ｭ繧ｰ' },
];

export default function AdminSidebar() {
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const router = useRouter();
  const [userEmail, setUserEmail] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [loggingOut, setLoggingOut] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(({ data: { user } }) => {
      setUserEmail(user?.email ?? null);
    });
  }, []);

  const handleLogout = async () => {
    setLoggingOut(true);
    await supabase.auth.signOut();
    router.push('/admin/login');
    router.refresh();
  };

  return (
    <aside className="w-56 shrink-0 border-r border-gray-200 bg-white min-h-screen flex flex-col">
      <div className="px-4 py-5 border-b border-gray-200">
        <h1 className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800 tracking-wide">
          繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ邂｡逅・
        </h1>
      </div>
      <nav className="mt-2 flex-1">
        <ul className="space-y-0.5 px-2">
          {menuItems.map((item) => {
            const isActive =
              item.href === '/admin'
                ? pathname === '/admin'
                : pathname.startsWith(item.href);

            return (
              <li key={item.href}>
                <Link
                  href={item.href}
                  className={`block px-3 py-2 rounded text-sm transition-colors ${
                    isActive
                      ? 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-900 font-medium'
                      : 'text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:text-gray-900'
                  }`}
                >
                  {item.label}
                </Link>
              </li>
            );
          })}
        </ul>
      </nav>

      {/* 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ迥ｶ諷九・繝ｭ繧ｰ繧｢繧ｦ繝・*/}
      <div className="border-t border-gray-200 px-4 py-3">
        {userEmail && (
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 truncate mb-2" title={userEmail}>
            {userEmail}
          </p>
        )}
        <button
          onClick={handleLogout}
          disabled={loggingOut}
          className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 rounded text-sm text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:text-gray-900 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          {loggingOut ? '繝ｭ繧ｰ繧｢繧ｦ繝井ｸｭ...' : '繝ｭ繧ｰ繧｢繧ｦ繝・}
        </button>
      </div>
    </aside>
  );
}

'use client';

import type { AdminPlan } from '@/types/admin';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface Props {
  plan: AdminPlan;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export default function PlanEditPanel({ plan, onClose }: Props) {
  const isNew = plan.id === '';
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ ...plan });

  const handleChange = (
    e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement | HTMLSelectElement>
  ) => {
    const { name, value, type } = e.target;
    setForm((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      [name]:
        type === 'number'
          ? Number(value)
          : type === 'checkbox'
            ? (e.target as HTMLInputElement).checked
            : value,
    }));
  };

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // TODO: Supabase 縺ｸ縺ｮ菫晏ｭ伜・逅・
    alert('菫晏ｭ伜・逅・・譛ｪ螳溯｣・〒縺呻ｼ・upabase 騾｣謳ｺ蠕後↓譛牙柑蛹厄ｼ・);
    onClose();
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-start justify-end">
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/20" onClick={onClose} />
      <div className="relative w-full max-w-lg bg-white h-full shadow-lg overflow-y-auto">
        <div className="sticky top-0 bg-white border-b border-gray-200 px-6 py-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-gray-900">
            {isNew ? '繝励Λ繝ｳ譁ｰ隕丈ｽ懈・' : '繝励Λ繝ｳ邱ｨ髮・}
          </h2>
          <button
            onClick={onClose}
            className="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 text-lg leading-none"
          >
            ﾃ・
          </button>
        </div>
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="px-6 py-4 space-y-4">
          <Field label="繝励Λ繝ｳ蜷・>
            <input
              type="text"
              name="name"
              value={form.name}
              onChange={handleChange}
              className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gray-400"
            />
          </Field>
          <Field label="隱ｬ譏・>
            <textarea
              name="description"
              value={form.description}
              onChange={handleChange}
              rows={3}
              className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gray-400"
            />
          </Field>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <Field label="蝓ｺ譛ｬ譁咎≡・亥・・・>
              <input
                type="number"
                name="basePrice"
                value={form.basePrice}
                onChange={handleChange}
                min={0}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gray-400"
              />
            </Field>
            <Field label="螳壼藤・亥錐・・>
              <input
                type="number"
                name="capacity"
                value={form.capacity}
                onChange={handleChange}
                min={1}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gray-400"
              />
            </Field>
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <Field label="雋ｩ螢ｲ髢句ｧ区律">
              <input
                type="date"
                name="salesStartDate"
                value={form.salesStartDate ?? ''}
                onChange={handleChange}

function Field({
  label,
  children,
}: {
  label: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return (
    <div>
      <label className="block text-xs font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1">
        {label}
      </label>
      {children}
    </div>
  );

'use client';

import type { SalesRule } from '@/types/admin';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface Props {
  rule: SalesRule;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export default function RuleEditPanel({ rule, onClose }: Props) {
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ ...rule });
  const [newClosedDate, setNewClosedDate] = useState('');

  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    setForm((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      [name]: Number(value),
    }));
  };

  const addClosedDate = () => {
    if (!newClosedDate || form.closedDates.includes(newClosedDate)) return;
    setForm((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      closedDates: [...prev.closedDates, newClosedDate].sort(),
    }));
    setNewClosedDate('');
  };

  const removeClosedDate = (date: string) => {
    setForm((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      closedDates: prev.closedDates.filter((d) => d !== date),
    }));
  };

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    alert('菫晏ｭ伜・逅・・譛ｪ螳溯｣・〒縺呻ｼ・upabase 騾｣謳ｺ蠕後↓譛牙柑蛹厄ｼ・);
    onClose();
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-start justify-end">
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/20" onClick={onClose} />
      <div className="relative w-full max-w-lg bg-white h-full shadow-lg overflow-y-auto">

                value={form.bookableFromDaysBefore}
                onChange={handleChange}
                min={1}

import { BookingContext } from "@/types/options";

  booking: BookingContext;

/** 譌･莉倥ｒyyyy/MM/dd蠖｢蠑上↓繝輔か繝ｼ繝槭ャ繝・*/
function formatDate(dateStr: string): string {
  const d = new Date(dateStr);
  const y = d.getFullYear();
  const m = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0");
  const day = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, "0");
  const weekdays = ["譌･", "譛・, "轣ｫ", "豌ｴ", "譛ｨ", "驥・, "蝨・];
  const w = weekdays[d.getDay()];
  return `${y}/${m}/${day}・・{w}・荏;
}

export default function BookingSummaryBar({ booking }: Props) {

    <div className="bg-white/80 backdrop-blur-sm border border-emerald-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 mb-6">

      </div>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-x-4 gap-y-1 text-sm text-gray-700">
        <div className="flex justify-between">
          <span className="text-gray-500">蛻ｩ逕ｨ譌･</span>

function formatEventDate(dateStr?: string): string {
  if (!dateStr) return "";
  const d = new Date(dateStr);
  const m = d.getMonth() + 1;
  const day = d.getDate();
  const h = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, "0");
  const min = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, "0");
  return `${m}/${day} ${h}:${min}縲彖;
}

  option,
  selection,
  onChangePeople,

      ? option.capacity - option.currentParticipants
      : undefined;

    remaining !== undefined

    <div
      className={`rounded-xl border-2 p-4 transition-all duration-200 ${
        isSelected
          ? "border-amber-400 bg-amber-50/50 shadow-sm"
          : "border-gray-100 bg-white hover:border-gray-200"
      }`}
    >
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3 mb-2">
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-800 text-base">{option.name}</h4>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1 leading-relaxed">
            {option.description}
          </p>
        </div>
        <div className="text-right shrink-0">
          <div className="text-amber-700 font-bold text-base">
            ﾂ･{option.price.toLocaleString()} / {option.unitLabel}

=== FILE: C:\Users\takam\Downloads\キャンプ場システム開発\VScode\campsite-booking\src\components\booking\QuantityStepper.tsx ===
"use client";

interface Props {
  label: string;
  value: number;
  min?: number;
  max: number;
  onChange: (value: number) => void;
}

export default function QuantityStepper({
  label,
  value,
  min = 0,
  max,
  onChange,
}: Props) {
  const decrement = () => {
    if (value > min) onChange(value - 1);
  };
  const increment = () => {
    if (value < max) onChange(value + 1);
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <span className="text-xs text-gray-500 min-w-[2rem]">{label}</span>
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={decrement}
        disabled={value <= min}
        className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full border border-gray-300 flex items-center justify-center text-gray-600 disabled:opacity-30 disabled:cursor-not-allowed hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors text-lg font-medium"
        aria-label={`${label}繧呈ｸ帙ｉ縺兪}
      >
        竏・
      </button>
      <span className="w-8 text-center font-semibold text-gray-800 tabular-nums">
        {value}
      </span>
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={increment}
        disabled={value >= max}
        className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full border border-emerald-400 bg-emerald-50 flex items-center justify-center text-emerald-700 disabled:opacity-30 disabled:cursor-not-allowed hover:bg-emerald-100 transition-colors text-lg font-medium"
        aria-label={`${label}繧貞｢励ｄ縺兪}
      >
        +
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

function priceLabel(option: OptionItem): string {
  switch (option.priceType) {
    case "per_unit":
      return `ﾂ･${option.price.toLocaleString()} / ${option.unitLabel}`;
    case "per_day":
      return `ﾂ･${option.price.toLocaleString()} / ${option.unitLabel}繝ｻ譌･`;
    case "fixed":
      return `ﾂ･${option.price.toLocaleString()}`;
    default:
      return `ﾂ･${option.price.toLocaleString()}`;
  }
}

function OptionImage({ src, alt }: { src?: string; alt: string }) {
  if (src) {
    return (
      <Image
        src={src}
        alt={alt}
        width={400}
        height={200}
        className="object-cover w-full h-full rounded-xl"
      />
    );
  }
  return (
    <div className="w-full h-full rounded-xl bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center">
      <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">逕ｻ蜒乗ｺ門ｙ荳ｭ</span>
    </div>
  );
}

"use client";

import { OptionItem, OptionSelection } from "@/types/options";

interface Props {
  selections: OptionSelection[];
  options: OptionItem[];
  totalAmount: number;
}

export default function SelectedOptionsSummary({
  selections,
  options,
  totalAmount,
}: Props) {
  const activeSelections = selections.filter((s) => s.subtotal > 0);
  const optionMap = new Map(options.map((o) => [o.id, o]));

  if (activeSelections.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="text-center py-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">
        繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ縺碁∈謚槭＆繧後※縺・∪縺帙ｓ
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      {activeSelections.map((sel) => {
        const opt = optionMap.get(sel.optionId);
        if (!opt) return null;

        let detail = "";
        if (opt.category === "rental") {
          if (opt.priceType === "per_day") {
            detail = `${sel.quantity}${opt.unitLabel} ﾃ・${sel.days}譌･`;
          } else {
            detail = `${sel.quantity}${opt.unitLabel}`;
          }
        } else {
          detail = `${sel.people}${opt.unitLabel}`;
        }

        return (
          <div
            key={sel.optionId}
            className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm"
          >
            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
              <span className="text-gray-700 font-medium">{opt.name}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-400 ml-2">{detail}</span>
            </div>
            <span className="font-semibold text-gray-800 shrink-0 ml-2">
              ﾂ･{sel.subtotal.toLocaleString()}
            </span>
          </div>
        );
      })}

      <div className="border-t border-gray-200 pt-2 mt-2 flex items-center justify-between">
        <span className="font-bold text-gray-800">繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ蜷郁ｨ・/span>
        <span className="font-bold text-lg text-emerald-700">
          ﾂ･{totalAmount.toLocaleString()}
        </span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import QRCode from 'qrcode';

interface QRCodeDisplayProps {
  value: string;
  size?: number;
}

export default function QRCodeDisplay({ value, size = 256 }: QRCodeDisplayProps) {
  const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (canvasRef.current) {
      QRCode.toCanvas(canvasRef.current, value, {
        width: size,
        margin: 2,
      });
    }
  }, [value, size]);

  return <canvas ref={canvasRef} />;
}

  getPaymentMethodLabel,
  getPaymentStatusLabel,

interface ReservationSummaryCardProps {
  reservation: ReservationDetail;
}

/** 譌･莉倥ｒ "YYYY/MM/DD・域屆譌･・・ 蠖｢蠑上↓繝輔か繝ｼ繝槭ャ繝・*/
function formatDate(dateStr: string): string {
  const date = new Date(dateStr);
  const weekdays = ['譌･', '譛・, '轣ｫ', '豌ｴ', '譛ｨ', '驥・, '蝨・];
  const y = date.getFullYear();
  const m = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
  const d = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  const w = weekdays[date.getDay()];
  return `${y}/${m}/${d}・・{w}・荏;
}

export default function ReservationSummaryCard({
  reservation,
}: ReservationSummaryCardProps) {
  const nights = calculateNights(
    reservation.checkInDate,
    reservation.checkOutDate
  );

  const items: { label: string; value: string | React.ReactNode }[] = [
    {
      label: '莠育ｴ・分蜿ｷ',
      value: (
        <span className="font-mono text-sm">
          {reservation.id.substring(0, 8).toUpperCase()}
        </span>
      ),
    },
    { label: '蛻ｩ逕ｨ閠・錐', value: reservation.userName },
    { label: '繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ', value: formatDate(reservation.checkInDate) },
    { label: '繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝・, value: formatDate(reservation.checkOutDate) },
    { label: '螳ｿ豕頑焚', value: `${nights}豕柿 },
    {
      label: '繧ｵ繧､繝・,
      value: `${reservation.siteNumber}・・{getSiteTypeLabel(reservation.siteType)}・荏,
    },
    { label: '莠ｺ謨ｰ', value: `${reservation.guests}蜷港 },
    {
      label: '謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・,
      value: getPaymentMethodLabel(reservation.paymentMethod),
    },
    {
      label: '豎ｺ貂育憾豕・,
      value: getPaymentStatusLabel(reservation.paymentStatus),
    },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="rounded-xl border border-gray-200 bg-white shadow-sm">
      {/* 繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-gray-100 px-5 py-4">

=== FILE: C:\Users\takam\Downloads\キャンプ場システム開発\VScode\campsite-booking\src\components\StripePayment.tsx ===
'use client';

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { loadStripe } from '@stripe/stripe-js';
import {
  Elements,
  PaymentElement,
  useStripe,
  useElements,
} from '@stripe/react-stripe-js';
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';

const stripePromise = loadStripe(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY!);

interface PaymentFormProps {
  amount: number;
  onSuccess: (reservationId: string) => void;
  onCancel: () => void;
}

function PaymentForm({ amount, onSuccess, onCancel }: PaymentFormProps) {
  const stripe = useStripe();
  const elements = useElements();
  const [processing, setProcessing] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleSubmit = async (event: React.FormEvent) => {
    event.preventDefault();

    if (!stripe || !elements) return;

    setProcessing(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      // 莠育ｴ・ｒ菴懈・
      const { data: reservation, error: reservationError } = await supabase
        .from('reservations')
        .insert({
          user_id: 'temp-user', // LIFF繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼID縺ｫ鄂ｮ縺肴鋤縺・
          site_id: 'site-1', // 驕ｸ謚槭＆繧後◆繧ｵ繧､繝・
          check_in_date: '2024-01-01', // 驕ｸ謚槭＆繧後◆譌･莉・
          check_out_date: '2024-01-02',
          total_guests: 2, // 驕ｸ謚槭＆繧後◆莠ｺ謨ｰ
          total_amount: amount,
          status: 'pending'
        })
        .select()
        .single();

      if (reservationError) throw reservationError;

      // Stripe豎ｺ貂・
      const { error: stripeError } = await stripe.confirmPayment({
        elements,
        confirmParams: {
          return_url: `${window.location.origin}/booking/confirmation?id=${reservation.id}`,
        },
      });

      if (stripeError) {
        setError(stripeError.message || '豎ｺ貂医↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆');
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setError('莠育ｴ・ｽ懈・縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆');
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setProcessing(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
      <PaymentElement />
      {error && (
        <div className="text-red-600 text-sm">{error}</div>
      )}
      <div className="flex gap-4">
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={onCancel}
          className="flex-1 bg-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-600 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded"
        >
          繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ
        </button>
        <button
          type="submit"
          disabled={!stripe || processing}
          className="flex-1 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700 disabled:bg-gray-400 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded"
        >
          {processing ? '蜃ｦ逅・ｸｭ...' : `ﾂ･${amount.toLocaleString()} 豎ｺ貂・}
        </button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
}

interface StripePaymentProps {
  amount: number;
  onSuccess: (reservationId: string) => void;
  onCancel: () => void;
}

export default function StripePayment({ amount, onSuccess, onCancel }: StripePaymentProps) {
  const [clientSecret, setClientSecret] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    // 繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・繧ｵ繧､繝峨〒PaymentIntent繧剃ｽ懈・
    fetch('/api/create-payment-intent', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ amount }),
    })
      .then((res) => res.json())
      .then((data) => setClientSecret(data.clientSecret));
  }, [amount]);

  if (!clientSecret) {
    return <div>豎ｺ貂域ュ蝣ｱ繧定ｪｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳ｭ...</div>;
  }

  return (
    <Elements stripe={stripePromise} options={{ clientSecret }}>
      <PaymentForm amount={amount} onSuccess={onSuccess} onCancel={onCancel} />
    </Elements>
  );
}

 * 莠育ｴ・ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ蜿門ｾ鈴未謨ｰ・亥ｰ・擂逧・↓Supabase謗･邯壹↓蟾ｮ縺玲崛縺茨ｼ・
 *

 * ```ts
 * const { data, error } = await supabase
 *   .from('reservations')
 *   .select(`
 *     *,
 *     profiles!reservations_user_id_fkey(full_name, email),
 *     sites!reservations_site_id_fkey(site_number, type, campgrounds(name)),
 *     payments(method, status),
 *     check_ins(check_in_time)
 *   `)
 *   .eq('id', reservationId)
 *   .single();
 * ```
 */
export async function fetchReservationById(
  reservationId: string
): Promise<ReservationDetail | null> {
  // 繝繝溘・螳溯｣・ 螳滄圀縺ｫ縺ｯSupabase縺九ｉ蜿門ｾ・
  // 繝阪ャ繝医Ρ繝ｼ繧ｯ驕・ｻｶ繧偵す繝溘Η繝ｬ繝ｼ繝・
  await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 500));

  return dummyReservations[reservationId] ?? null;
}

=== FILE: C:\Users\takam\Downloads\キャンプ場システム開発\VScode\campsite-booking\src\lib\admin\actionLog.ts ===
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import type { Json } from '@/types/database';

export type ActionType =
  | 'reservation_create'
  | 'reservation_update'
  | 'reservation_cancel'
  | 'import_execute'
  | 'plan_update'
  | 'site_update'
  | 'sales_rule_update';

export type TargetType =
  | 'reservation'
  | 'import_job'
  | 'plan'
  | 'site'
  | 'sales_rule';

export interface LogActionInput {
  adminEmail: string;
  actionType: ActionType;
  targetType: TargetType;
  targetId?: string;
  before?: Record<string, unknown> | null;
  after?: Record<string, unknown> | null;
}

export async function logAdminAction(input: LogActionInput) {
  const { error } = await supabase.from('admin_action_logs').insert({
    admin_email: input.adminEmail,
    action_type: input.actionType,
    target_type: input.targetType,
    target_id: input.targetId ?? null,
    before_json: (input.before as Json) ?? null,
    after_json: (input.after as Json) ?? null,
  });
  if (error) {
    console.error('[logAdminAction] Failed:', error.message);
  }
}

    .from('admin_action_logs')
    .select('*')
    .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    .limit(limit);

}

    .limit(50);

/**
 * 邂｡逅・・愛螳壹・繝ｫ繝代・
 *
 * 迴ｾ蝨ｨ縺ｯ迺ｰ蠅・､画焚 ADMIN_EMAILS 縺ｫ繧医ｋ allowlist 譁ｹ蠑上・
 * 蟆・擂 admin_users 繝・・繝悶Ν縺ｫ遘ｻ陦後☆繧句ｴ蜷医・
 * isAdminEmail() 縺ｮ荳ｭ霄ｫ繧・DB 繝ｫ繝・け繧｢繝・・縺ｫ蟾ｮ縺玲崛縺医ｋ縺縺代〒繧医＞縲・
 */

function getAdminEmails(): string[] {
  const raw = process.env.ADMIN_EMAILS ?? ''
  return raw
    .split(',')
    .map((e) => e.trim().toLowerCase())
    .filter(Boolean)
}

/**
 * 繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ縺檎ｮ｡逅・・allowlist 縺ｫ蜷ｫ縺ｾ繧後ｋ縺九ｒ蛻､螳壹☆繧九・
 */
export function isAdminEmail(email: string | undefined | null): boolean {
  if (!email) return false
  const allowlist = getAdminEmails()
  if (allowlist.length === 0) return false
  return allowlist.includes(email.toLowerCase())
}

import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import { generateQrToken } from '@/lib/generateQrToken';
import {
  validateReservation,
  formatAdminErrors,
  calculateNights,
} from '@/lib/validateReservation';

import { notifyReservationCreated } from '@/lib/admin/notificationLog';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type GuestReservationRow = Database['public']['Tables']['guest_reservations']['Row'];
type PaymentMethod = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_method'];
type PaymentStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_status'];

export interface AdminReservationInput {
  userName: string;
  userPhone: string;
  userEmail: string;
  checkInDate: string;   // YYYY-MM-DD
  checkOutDate: string;  // YYYY-MM-DD
  guests: number;
  siteNumber: string;

  paymentStatus: PaymentStatus;

  totalAmount: number;

/** 繝輔Ο繝ｳ繝医お繝ｳ繝牙・繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・医ヵ繧ｩ繝ｼ繝蜈･蜉帙・蝓ｺ譛ｬ繝√ぉ繝・け・・*/
export function validateAdminReservation(
  input: AdminReservationInput,
): string | null {
  if (!input.userName.trim()) return '莠育ｴ・・錐繧貞・蜉帙＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞';
  if (!input.siteNumber.trim()) return '繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ繧帝∈謚槭＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞';
  if (!input.checkInDate) return '繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･繧貞・蜉帙＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞';
  if (!input.checkOutDate) return '繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律繧貞・蜉帙＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞';
  if (input.checkOutDate <= input.checkInDate) {
    return '繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律縺ｯ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･繧医ｊ蠕後↓縺励※縺上□縺輔＞';
  }
  if (input.guests < 1) return '莠ｺ謨ｰ縺ｯ1莠ｺ莉･荳翫ｒ謖・ｮ壹＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞';
  if (input.totalAmount < 0) return '驥鷹｡阪・0莉･荳翫ｒ謖・ｮ壹＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞';
  return null;
}

/** 邂｡逅・・焔蜍穂ｺ育ｴ・ｒ菫晏ｭ・*/
export async function createAdminReservation(
  input: AdminReservationInput,
): Promise<AdminCreateResult> {
  // 1. 繝輔か繝ｼ繝繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ
  const formError = validateAdminReservation(input);
  if (formError) {
    return { success: false, error: formError };
  }

  // 2. 蜈ｱ騾壹ヰ繝ｪ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・磯㍾隍・・螳壼藤繝ｻ蛛懈ｭ｢繧ｵ繧､繝医↑縺ｩ・・
  const validation = await validateReservation({
    siteNumber: input.siteNumber,
    checkInDate: input.checkInDate,
    checkOutDate: input.checkOutDate,
    guests: input.guests,
    source: 'admin',
  });

  if (!validation.valid) {
    return { success: false, error: formatAdminErrors(validation.errors) };
  }

  // 3. 螳ｿ豕頑焚・亥・騾壹Θ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｪ繝・ぅ縺九ｉ・・
  const nights = calculateNights(input.checkInDate, input.checkOutDate);

  // 4. INSERT
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .insert({
      user_name: input.userName.trim(),
      user_phone: input.userPhone.trim() || null,
      user_email: input.userEmail.trim() || null,
      check_in_date: input.checkInDate,
      check_out_date: input.checkOutDate,
      nights,
      guests: input.guests,
      site_number: input.siteNumber,
      total_amount: input.totalAmount,
      status: 'confirmed' as const,
      payment_method: input.paymentMethod,
      payment_status: input.paymentStatus,
      qr_token: generateQrToken(),
      options_json: [],
      agreed_cancellation: true,
      agreed_terms: true,
      agreed_sns: false,
      special_requests: input.specialRequests.trim() || null,
    })
    .select()
    .single();

  if (error) {
    console.error('[createAdminReservation] Supabase error:', error);
    return {
      success: false,
      error: error.message ?? '莠育ｴ・・菫晏ｭ倥↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆',
    };
  }

  // 5. 謫堺ｽ懊Ο繧ｰ繝ｻ騾夂衍
  if (input.adminEmail) {
    await logAdminAction({
      adminEmail: input.adminEmail,
      actionType: 'reservation_create',
      targetType: 'reservation',
      targetId: data.id,
      after: {
        user_name: data.user_name,
        check_in_date: data.check_in_date,
        check_out_date: data.check_out_date,
        guests: data.guests,
        site_number: data.site_number,
      },
    });
  }

  await notifyReservationCreated(data.id, input.userEmail || null);

  return { success: true, reservation: data };
}

import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type GuestReservationRow = Database['public']['Tables']['guest_reservations']['Row'];
type ReservationStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['reservation_status'];

export interface ReservationListFilter {
  status?: ReservationStatus | 'all';
  checkInDate?: string; // YYYY-MM-DD
}

export interface FetchReservationsResult {
  data: GuestReservationRow[];
  error: string | null;
}

/**
 * 邂｡逅・判髱｢逕ｨ: guest_reservations 縺ｮ荳隕ｧ蜿門ｾ・
 * - 繝輔ぅ繝ｫ繧ｿ: 繧ｹ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ, 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･
 * - 繧ｽ繝ｼ繝・ created_at desc
 */
export async function fetchReservations(
  filter?: ReservationListFilter,
): Promise<FetchReservationsResult> {
  let query = supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .select('*')
    .order('created_at', { ascending: false });

  if (filter?.status && filter.status !== 'all') {
    query = query.eq('status', filter.status);
  }

  if (filter?.checkInDate) {
    query = query.eq('check_in_date', filter.checkInDate);
  }

  const { data, error } = await query;

  if (error) {
    return { data: [], error: error.message };
  }

  return { data: data ?? [], error: null };
}

 * 邂｡逅・判髱｢逕ｨ: guest_reservations 縺ｮ1莉ｶ蜿門ｾ・
 */
export async function fetchReservationByIdAdmin(
  id: string,
): Promise<{ data: GuestReservationRow | null; error: string | null }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .select('*')
    .eq('id', id)
    .single();

  if (error) {
    return { data: null, error: error.message };
  }

  return { data, error: null };
}
=== FILE: C:\Users\takam\Downloads\キャンプ場システム開発\VScode\campsite-booking\src\lib\admin\importParser.ts ===
import * as XLSX from 'xlsx';
import type {
  ImportRawRow,
  ImportParsedRow,
  ImportRowError,
  ImportDuplicate,
  ImportValidationResult,
} from '@/types/import';
import { REQUIRED_COLUMNS, PAYMENT_METHOD_MAP } from '@/types/import';
import { parseSiteNumber } from '@/lib/validateReservation';

// --- 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ繝代・繧ｹ ---

/** 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ(CSV/Excel)縺ｮArrayBuffer縺九ｉ繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ莉倥″陦碁・蛻励ｒ霑斐☆ */
export function parseFileToRows(
  buffer: ArrayBuffer,
  fileName: string,
): { rows: Record<string, string>[]; error?: string } {
  try {
    const workbook = XLSX.read(buffer, { type: 'array' });
    const sheetName = workbook.SheetNames[0];
    if (!sheetName) return { rows: [], error: '繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ' };

    const sheet = workbook.Sheets[sheetName];
    const jsonRows = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json<Record<string, string>>(sheet, {
      defval: '',
      raw: false,
    });

    return { rows: jsonRows };
  } catch {
    return {
      rows: [],
      error: `繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ縺ｮ隱ｭ縺ｿ蜿悶ｊ縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆: ${fileName}`,
    };
  }
}

/** 蠢・亥・縺後・繝・ム繝ｼ縺ｫ蜷ｫ縺ｾ繧後※縺・ｋ縺九メ繧ｧ繝・け */
export function checkRequiredColumns(
  headers: string[],
): { ok: boolean; missing: string[] } {
  const trimmed = headers.map((h) => h.trim());
  const missing = REQUIRED_COLUMNS.filter((col) => !trimmed.includes(col));
  return { ok: missing.length === 0, missing };
}

// --- 譌･莉倥ヱ繝ｼ繧ｹ ---

const DATE_REGEX_YYYY_MM_DD = /^\d{4}[-/]\d{1,2}[-/]\d{1,2}$/;

/** 譌･莉俶枚蟄怜・繧炭YYY-MM-DD蠖｢蠑上↓豁｣隕丞喧 */
function normalizeDate(raw: string): string | null {
  const trimmed = raw.trim();
  if (!trimmed) return null;

  // YYYY-MM-DD or YYYY/MM/DD
  if (DATE_REGEX_YYYY_MM_DD.test(trimmed)) {
    const parts = trimmed.split(/[-/]/);
    const y = parts[0];
    const m = parts[1].padStart(2, '0');
    const d = parts[2].padStart(2, '0');
    const dateStr = `${y}-${m}-${d}`;
    // 譛牙柑縺ｪ譌･莉倥°遒ｺ隱・
    const date = new Date(dateStr);
    if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return null;
    return dateStr;
  }

  // Excel縺ｮ繧ｷ繝ｪ繧｢繝ｫ譌･莉・謨ｰ蛟､)
  const num = Number(trimmed);
  if (!isNaN(num) && num > 30000 && num < 100000) {
    // Excel縺ｮ繧ｷ繝ｪ繧｢繝ｫ譌･莉倥ｒJS縺ｮDate縺ｫ螟画鋤
    const date = new Date((num - 25569) * 86400 * 1000);
    if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return null;
    const y = date.getUTCFullYear();
    const m = String(date.getUTCMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
    const d = String(date.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    return `${y}-${m}-${d}`;
  }

  return null;
}

// --- 陦後ヰ繝ｪ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ ---

/** 譛牙柑縺ｪ繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ繝ｪ繧ｹ繝茨ｼ医ム繝溘・繝・・繧ｿ縺九ｉ蜿門ｾ励ょｰ・擂逧・↓Supabase縺ｫ鄂ｮ縺肴鋤縺亥庄閭ｽ・・*/
const VALID_SITE_NUMBERS = ['A-01', 'A-02', 'B-01', 'B-02'];

/** 繧ｵ繧､繝亥ｮ壼藤繝槭ャ繝暦ｼ亥ｰ・擂逧・↓Supabase縺ｫ鄂ｮ縺肴鋤縺亥庄閭ｽ・・*/
const SITE_CAPACITY: Record<string, number> = {
  'A-01': 4,
  'A-02': 6,
  'B-01': 4,
  'B-02': 8,
};

/** 1陦後ｒ讀懆ｨｼ縺励※繝代・繧ｹ貂医∩陦・or 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ繧定ｿ斐☆ */
export function validateRow(
  raw: Record<string, string>,
  rowIndex: number,
  validSiteNumbers?: string[],
  siteCapacityMap?: Record<string, number>,
): { parsed?: ImportParsedRow; errors: string[] } {
  const errors: string[] = [];
  const sites = validSiteNumbers ?? VALID_SITE_NUMBERS;
  const capacities = siteCapacityMap ?? SITE_CAPACITY;

  const r: ImportRawRow = {
    莠育ｴ・・錐: (raw['莠育ｴ・・錐'] ?? '').trim(),
    髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ: (raw['髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ'] ?? '').trim(),
    繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ: (raw['繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ'] ?? '').trim(),
    繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･: (raw['繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･'] ?? '').trim(),
    繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律: (raw['繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律'] ?? '').trim(),
    莠ｺ謨ｰ: (raw['莠ｺ謨ｰ'] ?? '').trim(),
    繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ: (raw['繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ'] ?? '').trim(),
    謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・ (raw['謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・] ?? '').trim(),
    蛯呵・ (raw['蛯呵・] ?? '').trim(),
  };

  // 蠢・医メ繧ｧ繝・け
  if (!r.莠育ｴ・・錐) errors.push('莠育ｴ・・錐縺檎ｩｺ縺ｧ縺・);
  if (!r.髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ) errors.push('髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ縺檎ｩｺ縺ｧ縺・);
  if (!r.繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ) errors.push('繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ縺檎ｩｺ縺ｧ縺・);
  if (!r.繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･) errors.push('繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･縺檎ｩｺ縺ｧ縺・);
  if (!r.繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律) errors.push('繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律縺檎ｩｺ縺ｧ縺・);
  if (!r.莠ｺ謨ｰ) errors.push('莠ｺ謨ｰ縺檎ｩｺ縺ｧ縺・);
  if (!r.繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ) errors.push('繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ縺檎ｩｺ縺ｧ縺・);
  if (!r.謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・ errors.push('謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕輔′遨ｺ縺ｧ縺・);

  // 譌･莉・
  const checkInDate = normalizeDate(r.繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･);
  const checkOutDate = normalizeDate(r.繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律);

  if (r.繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･ && !checkInDate) {
    errors.push(`繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･縺ｮ蠖｢蠑上′荳肴ｭ｣縺ｧ縺・ "${r.繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･}"`);

    errors.push(`繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律縺ｮ蠖｢蠑上′荳肴ｭ｣縺ｧ縺・ "${r.繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律}"`);
  }
  if (checkInDate && checkOutDate && checkOutDate <= checkInDate) {
    errors.push('繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律縺ｯ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･繧医ｊ蠕後↓縺励※縺上□縺輔＞');

  const guests = parseInt(r.莠ｺ謨ｰ, 10);
  if (r.莠ｺ謨ｰ && (isNaN(guests) || guests < 1)) {
    errors.push(`莠ｺ謨ｰ縺御ｸ肴ｭ｣縺ｧ縺・ "${r.莠ｺ謨ｰ}"`);
  }

  // 繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ・・! 繝励Ξ繝輔ぅ繝・け繧ｹ蟇ｾ蠢懶ｼ・
  const { siteNumber: normalizedSite } = parseSiteNumber(r.繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ);

  if (r.繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ && !sites.includes(normalizedSite)) {
    errors.push(`繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ縺悟ｭ伜惠縺励∪縺帙ｓ: "${r.繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ}"`);
  }

  // 螳壼藤繝√ぉ繝・け

    const cap = capacities[normalizedSite];
    if (cap && guests > cap) {
      errors.push(`莠ｺ謨ｰ縺悟ｮ壼藤雜・℃縺ｧ縺・ ${guests}蜷搾ｼ亥ｮ壼藤${cap}蜷搾ｼ峨し繧､繝・${normalizedSite}`);
    }
  }

  // 謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・
  const paymentMethod = PAYMENT_METHOD_MAP[r.謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕評;
  if (r.謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・&& !paymentMethod) {
    errors.push(
      `謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕輔′荳肴ｭ｣縺ｧ縺・ "${r.謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕扶"・医け繝ｬ繧ｸ繝・ヨ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝・/ 迴ｾ蝨ｰ謇輔＞ / 驫陦梧険霎ｼ・荏,
    );
  }

  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return { errors };
  }

  return {
    parsed: {
      rowIndex,
      userName: r.莠育ｴ・・錐,
      userPhone: r.髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ,
      userEmail: r.繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ,
      checkInDate: checkInDate!,
      checkOutDate: checkOutDate!,
      guests: guests,
      siteNumber: normalizedSite,
      paymentMethod: paymentMethod!,
      specialRequests: r.蛯呵・
    },
    errors: [],
  };
}

// --- 驥崎､・メ繧ｧ繝・け ---

export interface ExistingReservation {
  site_number: string;
  check_in_date: string;
  check_out_date: string;
}

/** 繝代・繧ｹ貂医∩陦後→譌｢蟄倅ｺ育ｴ・ｒ遯√″蜷医ｏ縺帙※驥崎､・ｒ讀懷・ */
export function detectDuplicates(
  validRows: ImportParsedRow[],
  existingReservations: ExistingReservation[],
): { clean: ImportParsedRow[]; duplicates: ImportDuplicate[] } {
  const clean: ImportParsedRow[] = [];
  const duplicates: ImportDuplicate[] = [];

  for (const row of validRows) {
    const overlap = existingReservations.find(
      (e) =>
        e.site_number === row.siteNumber &&
        e.check_in_date < row.checkOutDate &&
        e.check_out_date > row.checkInDate,
    );

    if (overlap) {
      duplicates.push({
        rowIndex: row.rowIndex,
        parsed: row,
        existingCheckIn: overlap.check_in_date,
        existingCheckOut: overlap.check_out_date,
      });
    } else {
      clean.push(row);
    }
  }

  return { clean, duplicates };
}

/** 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ蜀・〒縺ｮ陦悟酔螢ｫ縺ｮ驥崎､・ｂ繝√ぉ繝・け */
export function detectInternalDuplicates(
  rows: ImportParsedRow[],
): { clean: ImportParsedRow[]; duplicates: ImportDuplicate[] } {
  const clean: ImportParsedRow[] = [];
  const duplicates: ImportDuplicate[] = [];

  for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    const row = rows[i];
    // 蜈医↓霑ｽ蜉貂医∩縺ｮ陦後→驥崎､・☆繧九°繝√ぉ繝・け
    const overlapWith = clean.find(
      (c) =>
        c.siteNumber === row.siteNumber &&
        c.checkInDate < row.checkOutDate &&
        c.checkOutDate > row.checkInDate,
    );

    if (overlapWith) {
      duplicates.push({
        rowIndex: row.rowIndex,
        parsed: row,
        existingCheckIn: overlapWith.checkInDate,
        existingCheckOut: overlapWith.checkOutDate,
      });
    } else {
      clean.push(row);
    }
  }

  return { clean, duplicates };
}

// --- 蜈ｨ菴捺､懆ｨｼ ---

export function validateAllRows(
  rawRows: Record<string, string>[],
  existingReservations: ExistingReservation[],
  validSiteNumbers?: string[],
  siteCapacityMap?: Record<string, number>,
): ImportValidationResult {
  const validRows: ImportParsedRow[] = [];
  const errorRows: ImportRowError[] = [];

  for (let i = 0; i < rawRows.length; i++) {
    const raw = rawRows[i];
    const { parsed, errors } = validateRow(raw, i + 1, validSiteNumbers, siteCapacityMap);

    if (errors.length > 0) {
      errorRows.push({
        rowIndex: i + 1,
        raw: {
          莠育ｴ・・錐: (raw['莠育ｴ・・錐'] ?? '').trim(),
          髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ: (raw['髮ｻ隧ｱ逡ｪ蜿ｷ'] ?? '').trim(),
          繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ: (raw['繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ繧｢繝峨Ξ繧ｹ'] ?? '').trim(),
          繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･: (raw['繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･'] ?? '').trim(),
          繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律: (raw['繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律'] ?? '').trim(),
          莠ｺ謨ｰ: (raw['莠ｺ謨ｰ'] ?? '').trim(),
          繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ: (raw['繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ'] ?? '').trim(),
          謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・ (raw['謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕・] ?? '').trim(),
          蛯呵・ (raw['蛯呵・] ?? '').trim(),
        },
        errors,
      });
    } else if (parsed) {
      validRows.push(parsed);
    }
  }

  // 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ蜀・㍾隍・メ繧ｧ繝・け
  const internal = detectInternalDuplicates(validRows);

  // 譌｢蟄倅ｺ育ｴ・→縺ｮ驥崎､・メ繧ｧ繝・け
  const external = detectDuplicates(internal.clean, existingReservations);

  return {
    validRows: external.clean,
    errorRows,
    duplicateRows: [...internal.duplicates, ...external.duplicates],
  };
}

  reservationId?: string;
  type: NotificationType;
  channel: NotificationChannel;
  recipient?: string;

/**
 * 騾夂衍繝ｭ繧ｰ繧・莉ｶ險倬鹸縺吶ｋ縲・
 * 迴ｾ譎らせ縺ｧ縺ｯ螳滄圀縺ｮ騾∽ｿ｡縺ｯ陦後ｏ縺壹《tatus='queued' 縺ｧ菫晏ｭ倥・

export async function createNotificationLog(input: CreateNotificationInput) {

    reservation_id: input.reservationId ?? null,
    notification_type: input.type,
    channel: input.channel,
    recipient: input.recipient ?? null,
    payload_json: (input.payload as Json) ?? {},
    status: 'queued',
  });

    console.error('[createNotificationLog] Failed:', error.message);

import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import {
  validateReservation,
  formatAdminErrors,
  calculateNights,
} from '@/lib/validateReservation';
import { logAdminAction } from '@/lib/admin/actionLog';
import {
  notifyReservationUpdated,
  notifyReservationCancelled,
} from '@/lib/admin/notificationLog';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type GuestReservationRow = Database['public']['Tables']['guest_reservations']['Row'];
type PaymentMethod = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_method'];
type PaymentStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_status'];

export interface UpdateReservationInput {
  checkInDate: string;
  checkOutDate: string;
  guests: number;
  adults: number;
  children: number;
  infants: number;
  pets: number;
  cars: number;
  siteNumber: string;
  specialRequests: string;
  paymentMethod: PaymentMethod;
  paymentStatus: PaymentStatus;
  totalAmount: number;
}

export type UpdateResult =
  | { success: true; reservation: GuestReservationRow }
  | { success: false; error: string };

/**
 * 邂｡逅・・↓繧医ｋ莠育ｴ・､画峩
 */
export async function updateReservation(
  id: string,
  input: UpdateReservationInput,
  adminEmail: string,
): Promise<UpdateResult> {
  // 1. 迴ｾ蝨ｨ縺ｮ莠育ｴ・ｒ蜿門ｾ・
  const { data: current, error: fetchErr } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .select('*')
    .eq('id', id)
    .single();

  if (fetchErr || !current) {
    return { success: false, error: '莠育ｴ・′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ' };
  }

  if (current.status === 'cancelled') {
    return { success: false, error: '繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ貂医∩縺ｮ莠育ｴ・・螟画峩縺ｧ縺阪∪縺帙ｓ' };
  }

  // 2. 蝓ｺ譛ｬ繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ
  if (input.checkOutDate <= input.checkInDate) {
    return { success: false, error: '繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律縺ｯ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･繧医ｊ蠕後↓縺励※縺上□縺輔＞' };
  }
  if (input.guests < 1) {
    return { success: false, error: '莠ｺ謨ｰ縺ｯ1莠ｺ莉･荳翫ｒ謖・ｮ壹＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞' };
  }

  // 3. 蜈ｱ騾壹ヰ繝ｪ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・磯㍾隍・メ繧ｧ繝・け譎ゅ↓閾ｪ蛻・・霄ｫ繧帝勁螟厄ｼ・
  const validation = await validateReservation({
    siteNumber: input.siteNumber,
    checkInDate: input.checkInDate,
    checkOutDate: input.checkOutDate,
    guests: input.guests,
    source: 'admin_update',
    excludeReservationId: id,
  });

  if (!validation.valid) {
    return { success: false, error: formatAdminErrors(validation.errors) };
  }

  const nights = calculateNights(input.checkInDate, input.checkOutDate);

  // 4. UPDATE
  const { data: updated, error: updateErr } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .update({
      check_in_date: input.checkInDate,
      check_out_date: input.checkOutDate,
      nights,
      guests: input.guests,
      adults: input.adults,
      children: input.children,
      infants: input.infants,
      pets: input.pets,
      cars: input.cars,
      site_number: input.siteNumber,
      special_requests: input.specialRequests.trim() || null,
      payment_method: input.paymentMethod,
      payment_status: input.paymentStatus,
      total_amount: input.totalAmount,
    })
    .eq('id', id)
    .select()
    .single();

  if (updateErr) {
    return { success: false, error: updateErr.message };
  }

  // 5. 螟画峩蜑榊ｾ後・蟾ｮ蛻・ｒ邂怜・縺励※繝ｭ繧ｰ
  const changes = buildChanges(current, updated);

  await logAdminAction({
    adminEmail,
    actionType: 'reservation_update',
    targetType: 'reservation',
    targetId: id,
    before: pickFields(current),
    after: pickFields(updated),
  });

  // 6. 騾夂衍險倬鹸
  await notifyReservationUpdated(id, current.user_email, changes);

  return { success: true, reservation: updated };
}

/**
 * 邂｡逅・・↓繧医ｋ莠育ｴ・く繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ
 */
export async function cancelReservation(
  id: string,
  adminEmail: string,
): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }> {
  // 1. 迴ｾ蝨ｨ縺ｮ莠育ｴ・ｒ蜿門ｾ・
  const { data: current, error: fetchErr } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .select('*')
    .eq('id', id)
    .single();

  if (fetchErr || !current) {
    return { success: false, error: '莠育ｴ・′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ' };
  }

  if (current.status === 'cancelled') {
    return { success: false, error: '縺吶〒縺ｫ繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ貂医∩縺ｧ縺・ };
  }

  // 2. 繧ｹ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ繧・cancelled 縺ｫ螟画峩
  const { error: updateErr } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .update({ status: 'cancelled' })
    .eq('id', id);

  if (updateErr) {
    return { success: false, error: updateErr.message };
  }

  // 3. 謫堺ｽ懊Ο繧ｰ
  await logAdminAction({
    adminEmail,
    actionType: 'reservation_cancel',
    targetType: 'reservation',
    targetId: id,
    before: pickFields(current),
    after: { ...pickFields(current), status: 'cancelled' },
  });

  // 4. 騾夂衍險倬鹸
  await notifyReservationCancelled(id, current.user_email);

  return { success: true };
}

// --- 蜀・Κ繝ｦ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｪ繝・ぅ ---

function pickFields(r: GuestReservationRow): Record<string, unknown> {
  return {
    check_in_date: r.check_in_date,
    check_out_date: r.check_out_date,
    nights: r.nights,
    guests: r.guests,
    adults: r.adults,
    children: r.children,
    infants: r.infants,
    pets: r.pets,
    cars: r.cars,
    site_number: r.site_number,
    special_requests: r.special_requests,
    payment_method: r.payment_method,
    payment_status: r.payment_status,
    total_amount: r.total_amount,
    status: r.status,
  };
}

function buildChanges(
  before: GuestReservationRow,
  after: GuestReservationRow,
): Record<string, unknown> {
  const changes: Record<string, unknown> = {};
  const keys = [
    'check_in_date', 'check_out_date', 'guests', 'adults', 'children',
    'infants', 'pets', 'cars', 'site_number',
    'special_requests', 'payment_method', 'payment_status', 'total_amount',
  ] as const;

  for (const key of keys) {
    const b = before[key];
    const a = after[key];
    if (String(b) !== String(a)) {
      changes[key] = { from: b, to: a };
    }
  }
  return changes;
}
=== FILE: C:\Users\takam\Downloads\キャンプ場システム開発\VScode\campsite-booking\src\lib\bookingToReservation.ts ===
import type { BookingDraft } from '@/stores/bookingDraftStore';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type GuestReservationInsert = Database['public']['Tables']['guest_reservations']['Insert'];
type PaymentMethod = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_method'];
type PaymentStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_status'];
type ReservationStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['reservation_status'];

/**
 * bookingDraft 縺ｮ payment.method 竊・DB 縺ｮ payment_method enum 縺ｸ螟画鋤
 */
function toDbPaymentMethod(method: BookingDraft['payment']['method']): PaymentMethod | null {
  if (method === 'credit_card') return 'credit_card';
  if (method === 'on_site') return 'cash';
  return null;
}

/**
 * 謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕輔°繧峨せ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ蛻晄悄蛟､繧貞ｰ主・
 */
function deriveStatuses(method: BookingDraft['payment']['method']): {
  reservationStatus: ReservationStatus;
  paymentStatus: PaymentStatus;
} {
  if (method === 'credit_card') {
    return { reservationStatus: 'confirmed', paymentStatus: 'paid' };
  }
  // 迴ｾ蝨ｰ豎ｺ貂・
  return { reservationStatus: 'confirmed', paymentStatus: 'pending' };
}

/**
 * 繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ諠・ｱ繧・JSON 菫晏ｭ倡畑縺ｫ螟画鋤
 * 蠕後°繧・reservation_options 繝・・繝悶Ν縺ｸ蛻・ｊ蜃ｺ縺励ｄ縺吶＞蠖｢蠑・
 */
function buildOptionsJson(options: BookingDraft['options']) {
  const items: Array<{
    type: 'rental' | 'event';
    optionId: string;
    quantity: number;
    days?: number;
    people?: number;
    subtotal: number;
  }> = [];

  for (const r of options.rentals) {
    items.push({
      type: 'rental',
      optionId: r.optionId,
      quantity: r.quantity,
      days: r.days,
      subtotal: r.subtotal,
    });
  }

  for (const e of options.events) {
    items.push({
      type: 'event',
      optionId: e.optionId,
      quantity: 1,
      people: e.people,
      subtotal: e.subtotal,
    });
  }

  return items;
}

export interface BookingToReservationInput {
  draft: BookingDraft;
  qrToken: string;
  totalAmount: number;
}

/**
 * BookingDraft 竊・guest_reservations INSERT payload 縺ｸ螟画鋤
 */
export function bookingToReservation({
  draft,
  qrToken,
  totalAmount,
}: BookingToReservationInput): GuestReservationInsert {

import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

type GuestReservationInsert = Database['public']['Tables']['guest_reservations']['Insert'];
type GuestReservationRow = Database['public']['Tables']['guest_reservations']['Row'];

export type CreateReservationResult =
  | { success: true; reservation: GuestReservationRow }
  | { success: false; error: string };

/**
 * guest_reservations 繝・・繝悶Ν縺ｸ 1 莉ｶ INSERT
 */
export async function createReservation(
  payload: GuestReservationInsert,
): Promise<CreateReservationResult> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .insert(payload)
    .select()
    .single();

  if (error) {
    console.error('[createReservation] Supabase error:', error);
    return {
      success: false,
      error: error.message ?? '莠育ｴ・・菫晏ｭ倥↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆',
    };
  }

  return { success: true, reservation: data };
}

import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';
import type { ReservationDetail } from '@/types/reservation';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';
import { dummyReservations } from '@/data/reservationDummyData';

type GuestReservationRow = Database['public']['Tables']['guest_reservations']['Row'];

/**
 * guest_reservations 縺ｮ陦・竊・ReservationDetail 縺ｸ螟画鋤
 */
function toReservationDetail(row: GuestReservationRow): ReservationDetail {
  return {
    id: row.id,
    status: row.status,
    checkInDate: row.check_in_date,
    checkOutDate: row.check_out_date,
    guests: row.guests,
    totalAmount: Number(row.total_amount),
    specialRequests: row.special_requests,
    createdAt: row.created_at,
    qrToken: row.qr_token,
    checkedInAt: row.checked_in_at,
    userName: row.user_name,
    userEmail: row.user_email ?? '',
    siteNumber: row.site_number ?? '譛ｪ螳・,
    siteType: row.site_type,
    campgroundName: row.campground_name ?? '譽ｮ縺ｮ繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ Green Valley',
    paymentMethod: row.payment_method,
    paymentStatus: row.payment_status,
  };
}

/**
 * 莠育ｴИD縺ｧ蜿門ｾ・
 * 1. Supabase 縺ｮ guest_reservations 繧呈､懃ｴ｢
 * 2. 隕九▽縺九ｉ縺ｪ縺代ｌ縺ｰ譌｢蟄倥・繝繝溘・繝・・繧ｿ縺ｫ繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ
 */
export async function fetchReservationById(
  reservationId: string,
): Promise<ReservationDetail | null> {
  // Supabase 縺九ｉ蜿門ｾ・
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .select('*')
    .eq('id', reservationId)
    .single();

  if (!error && data) {
    return toReservationDetail(data);
  }

  // 繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ: 繝繝溘・繝・・繧ｿ
  return dummyReservations[reservationId] ?? null;
}

export const initializeLiff = async (liffId: string) => {

    await liff.init({ liffId });
    return liff;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('LIFF initialization failed', error);
    throw error;
  }

export const getLiffProfile = async () => {
  if (!liff.isLoggedIn()) {
    throw new Error('User not logged in to LIFF');
  }
  return await liff.getProfile();
};

export const loginWithLiff = () => {
  // 繝繝溘・ID縺ｮ蝣ｴ蜷医・繝・Δ繝｢繝ｼ繝峨→縺励※菴輔ｂ縺励↑縺・

    return;

    liff.login();
  }
};

import { createServerClient } from '@supabase/ssr';
import { cookies } from 'next/headers';
import type { Database } from '@/types/database';

/**
 * Server Component / Route Handler 蜷代￠ Supabase 繧ｯ繝ｩ繧､繧｢繝ｳ繝・
 */
export async function createSupabaseServerClient() {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();

  return createServerClient<Database>(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        getAll() {
          return cookieStore.getAll();
        },
        setAll(cookiesToSet) {
          try {
            cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value, options }) =>
              cookieStore.set(name, value, options),
            );
          } catch {
            // Server Component 縺九ｉ蜻ｼ縺ｰ繧後◆蝣ｴ蜷・set 縺ｯ辟｡隕悶＆繧後ｋ
          }
        },
      },
    },
  );
}

const tomorrow = (() => {
  const d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1);
  return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
})();

const dayAfterTomorrow = (() => {

  d.setDate(d.getDate() + 2);
  return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);

// 笏笏笏 繝・せ繝亥ｮ溯｡・笏笏笏

interface TestResult {
  name: string;
  passed: boolean;
  expected: string;
  actual: string;
  errors: string[];
}

/**
 * 蜈ｨ繝・せ繝医こ繝ｼ繧ｹ繧貞ｮ溯｡後＠縺ｦ繝ｬ繝昴・繝医ｒ霑斐☆縲・
 *
 * 繝悶Λ繧ｦ繧ｶ繧ｳ繝ｳ繧ｽ繝ｼ繝ｫ繧・ｮ｡逅・判髱｢縺ｮ繝・ヰ繝・げ逕ｨ縲・
 * 譛ｬ逡ｪ繝・・繝ｭ繧､蜑阪↓ `runValidationSuite()` 繧貞ｮ溯｡後＠縺ｦ蜈ｨ繝代せ縺吶ｋ縺薙→繧堤｢ｺ隱阪☆繧九・
 */
export async function runValidationSuite(): Promise<TestResult[]> {
  const results: TestResult[] = [];

  for (const tc of testFixtures) {
    const validation = await validateReservation(tc.input);
    const passed =
      validation.valid === tc.expectValid &&
      (!tc.expectCode || validation.errors.some((e) => e.code === tc.expectCode));

    results.push({
      name: tc.name,
      passed,
      expected: tc.expectValid ? 'valid' : `error(${tc.expectCode ?? 'any'})`,
      actual: validation.valid
        ? 'valid'
        : `error(${validation.errors.map((e) => e.code).join(',')})`,
      errors: validation.errors.map((e) => e.message),
    });
  }

  return results;
}

/**
 * 繝・せ繝育ｵ先棡縺ｮ繧ｵ繝槭Μ繝ｼ繧呈枚蟄怜・縺ｧ霑斐☆
 */
export function formatTestReport(results: TestResult[]): string {
  const passed = results.filter((r) => r.passed).length;
  const failed = results.filter((r) => !r.passed).length;
  const lines = [
    `繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繝・せ繝・ ${passed}/${results.length} 騾夐℃ (螟ｱ謨・ ${failed})`,
    '',
  ];

  for (const r of results) {
    const mark = r.passed ? 'OK' : 'NG';
    lines.push(`[${mark}] ${r.name}`);
    if (!r.passed) {
      lines.push(`  譛溷ｾ・ ${r.expected}`);
      lines.push(`  螳滄圀: ${r.actual}`);
    }
  }

  return lines.join('\n');
}

export interface ReservationValidationInput {

  checkOutDate: string; // YYYY-MM-DD
  guests: number;

}

// 笏笏笏 繝ｦ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｪ繝・ぅ 笏笏笏

/**
 * 蜈ｨ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ繧ｳ繝ｼ繝我ｸ隕ｧ
 *
 * 蜈ｨ邨瑚ｷｯ縺ｧ菴ｿ逕ｨ縺輔ｌ繧句・騾壹お繝ｩ繝ｼ繧ｳ繝ｼ繝峨・

 */
export const VALIDATION_ERROR_CODES = {
  INVALID_DATE_ORDER: 'INVALID_DATE_ORDER',
  INVALID_DATE_RANGE: 'INVALID_DATE_RANGE',
  MIN_NIGHTS: 'MIN_NIGHTS',
  MAX_NIGHTS: 'MAX_NIGHTS',
  INVALID_GUESTS: 'INVALID_GUESTS',
  SITE_NOT_FOUND: 'SITE_NOT_FOUND',
  SITE_NOT_PUBLISHED: 'SITE_NOT_PUBLISHED',
  SITE_UNAVAILABLE: 'SITE_UNAVAILABLE',
  CAPACITY_EXCEEDED: 'CAPACITY_EXCEEDED',
  PLAN_NOT_PUBLISHED: 'PLAN_NOT_PUBLISHED',
  BOOKING_OUTSIDE_WINDOW: 'BOOKING_OUTSIDE_WINDOW',
  BOOKING_TOO_EARLY: 'BOOKING_TOO_EARLY',
  BOOKING_TOO_LATE: 'BOOKING_TOO_LATE',
  CLOSED_DATE: 'CLOSED_DATE',
  SITE_CLOSED_DATE: 'SITE_CLOSED_DATE',
  DUPLICATE_RESERVATION: 'DUPLICATE_RESERVATION',
  OVERLAP_CHECK_ERROR: 'OVERLAP_CHECK_ERROR',
  UNKNOWN_ERROR: 'UNKNOWN_ERROR',
} as const;

export type ValidationErrorCode = typeof VALIDATION_ERROR_CODES[keyof typeof VALIDATION_ERROR_CODES];

  UNKNOWN_ERROR: '莠育ｴ・・逅・ｸｭ縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲・,
