/** YYYY-MM-DD譁・ｭ怜・ 竊・Date・・TC・・*/
function toDate(dateStr: string): Date {
  return new Date(dateStr + 'T00:00:00Z');
}

/** 螳ｿ豕頑焚繧定ｨ育ｮ・*/
export function calculateNights(checkIn: string, checkOut: string): number {
  const d1 = toDate(checkIn);
  const d2 = toDate(checkOut);
  return Math.ceil((d2.getTime() - d1.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
}

/** 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･ + 豕頑焚 竊・繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律繧貞ｰ主・ */
export function deriveCheckOutDate(checkIn: string, nights: number): string {
  const d = toDate(checkIn);
  d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + nights);
  const y = d.getUTCFullYear();
  const m = String(d.getUTCMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
  const day = String(d.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  return `${y}-${m}-${day}`;
}

/**
 * 繧ｵ繧､繝育分蜿ｷ縺ｮ `!` 繝励Ξ繝輔ぅ繝・け繧ｹ繧定ｧ｣驥・
 * "!A-01" 竊・{ siteNumber: "A-01", designationRequested: true }
 * "A-01"  竊・{ siteNumber: "A-01", designationRequested: false }
 */
export function parseSiteNumber(raw: string): {
  siteNumber: string;
  designationRequested: boolean;
} {
  const trimmed = raw.trim();
  if (trimmed.startsWith('!')) {
    return { siteNumber: trimmed.slice(1), designationRequested: true };
  }
  return { siteNumber: trimmed, designationRequested: false };
}

/**
 * 謖・ｮ壽律髢薙↓蜷ｫ縺ｾ繧後ｋ縺吶∋縺ｦ縺ｮ螳ｿ豕頑律繧貞・謖・
 * 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･ 縲・繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝亥燕譌･
 */
function getStayDates(checkIn: string, checkOut: string): string[] {
  const dates: string[] = [];
  const start = toDate(checkIn);
  const end = toDate(checkOut);
  const cursor = new Date(start);
  while (cursor < end) {
    const y = cursor.getUTCFullYear();
    const m = String(cursor.getUTCMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
    const d = String(cursor.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    dates.push(`${y}-${m}-${d}`);
    cursor.setUTCDate(cursor.getUTCDate() + 1);
  }
  return dates;
}

// 笏笏笏 蛟句挨繝√ぉ繝・け髢｢謨ｰ 笏笏笏

function checkDateOrder(input: ReservationValidationInput): ValidationError | null {
  if (input.checkOutDate <= input.checkInDate) {
    return {
      code: 'INVALID_DATE_ORDER',
      message: '繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝域律縺ｯ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譌･繧医ｊ蠕後ｒ謖・ｮ壹＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・,
      adminMessage: `譌･莉倬・ｺ上お繝ｩ繝ｼ: 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ=${input.checkInDate}, 繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝・${input.checkOutDate}`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkNightsRange(nights: number): ValidationError | null {
  const { minNights, maxNights } = dummySalesRule;
  if (nights < minNights) {
    return {
      code: 'MIN_NIGHTS',
      message: `譛菴・{minNights}豕贋ｻ･荳翫・莠育ｴ・′蠢・ｦ√〒縺吶Ａ,
      adminMessage: `豕頑焚荳崎ｶｳ: ${nights}豕・(譛菴・{minNights}豕・`,
    };
  }
  if (nights > maxNights) {
    return {
      code: 'MAX_NIGHTS',
      message: `譛螟ｧ${maxNights}豕翫∪縺ｧ縺ｮ莠育ｴ・′蜿ｯ閭ｽ縺ｧ縺吶Ａ,
      adminMessage: `豕頑焚雜・℃: ${nights}豕・(譛螟ｧ${maxNights}豕・`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkGuestsPositive(guests: number): ValidationError | null {
  if (guests < 1) {
    return {
      code: 'INVALID_GUESTS',
      message: '莠ｺ謨ｰ縺ｯ1莠ｺ莉･荳翫ｒ謖・ｮ壹＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・,
      adminMessage: `莠ｺ謨ｰ荳肴ｭ｣: ${guests}`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkSiteExists(siteNumber: string): ValidationError | null {
  const site = dummySites.find((s) => s.siteNumber === siteNumber);
  if (!site) {
    return {
      code: 'SITE_NOT_FOUND',
      message: '謖・ｮ壹＆繧後◆繧ｵ繧､繝医′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・,
      adminMessage: `繧ｵ繧､繝・"${siteNumber}" 縺ｯ繝槭せ繧ｿ縺ｫ蟄伜惠縺励∪縺帙ｓ`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkSitePublished(
  siteNumber: string,
  source: ReservationSource,
): ValidationError | null {
  // 邂｡逅・・・繧､繝ｳ繝昴・繝医・邂｡逅・峩譁ｰ縺ｯ髱槫・髢九し繧､繝医∈縺ｮ莠育ｴ・ｒ險ｱ蜿ｯ
  if (source !== 'web') return null;

  const site = dummySites.find((s) => s.siteNumber === siteNumber);
  if (site && !site.isPublished) {
    return {
      code: 'SITE_NOT_PUBLISHED',
      message: '縺薙・繧ｵ繧､繝医・迴ｾ蝨ｨ蜈ｬ髢九＆繧後※縺・∪縺帙ｓ縲・,
      adminMessage: `繧ｵ繧､繝・"${siteNumber}" 縺ｯ髱槫・髢・(isPublished=false)`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkSiteStatus(siteNumber: string): ValidationError | null {
  const site = dummySites.find((s) => s.siteNumber === siteNumber);
  if (!site) return null; // checkSiteExists 縺ｧ蠑輔▲縺九°繧・

  if (site.status === 'closed') {
    return {
      code: 'SITE_UNAVAILABLE',
      message: '縺薙・繧ｵ繧､繝医・蛻ｩ逕ｨ蛛懈ｭ｢荳ｭ縺ｧ縺吶・,
      adminMessage: `繧ｵ繧､繝・"${siteNumber}" 縺ｯ蛻ｩ逕ｨ蛛懈ｭ｢ (status=closed)`,
    };
  }
  if (site.status === 'maintenance') {
    return {
      code: 'SITE_UNAVAILABLE',
      message: '縺薙・繧ｵ繧､繝医・繝｡繝ｳ繝・リ繝ｳ繧ｹ荳ｭ縺ｧ縺吶・,
      adminMessage: `繧ｵ繧､繝・"${siteNumber}" 縺ｯ繝｡繝ｳ繝・リ繝ｳ繧ｹ荳ｭ (status=maintenance)`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkCapacity(siteNumber: string, guests: number): ValidationError | null {
  const site = dummySites.find((s) => s.siteNumber === siteNumber);
  if (!site) return null;

  if (guests > site.capacity) {
    return {
      code: 'CAPACITY_EXCEEDED',
      message: `縺薙・繧ｵ繧､繝医・螳壼藤縺ｯ${site.capacity}蜷阪∪縺ｧ縺ｧ縺吶Ａ,
      adminMessage: `螳壼藤雜・℃: ${guests}蜷・> 螳壼藤${site.capacity}蜷・(繧ｵ繧､繝・${siteNumber})`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkPlanPublished(
  planId: string | null | undefined,
  source: ReservationSource,
): ValidationError | null {
  // 邂｡逅・・・繧､繝ｳ繝昴・繝医・繧ｹ繧ｭ繝・・ / 繝励Λ繝ｳ縺梧悴謖・ｮ壹ｂ繧ｹ繧ｭ繝・・
  if (source !== 'web' || !planId) return null;

  const plan = dummyPlans.find((p) => p.id === planId);
  if (plan && !plan.isPublished) {
    return {
      code: 'PLAN_NOT_PUBLISHED',
      message: '縺薙・繝励Λ繝ｳ縺ｯ迴ｾ蝨ｨ蜈ｬ髢九＆繧後※縺・∪縺帙ｓ縲・,
      adminMessage: `繝励Λ繝ｳ "${plan.name}" (${planId}) 縺ｯ髱槫・髢義,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkBookingPeriod(
  checkInDate: string,
  source: ReservationSource,
): ValidationError | null {
  // 邂｡逅・・・邂｡逅・峩譁ｰ縺ｯ蜿嶺ｻ俶悄髢灘､悶〒繧ら匳骭ｲ蜿ｯ閭ｽ
  if (source === 'admin' || source === 'admin_update') return null;

  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const checkIn = new Date(checkInDate + 'T00:00:00');

  const diffDays = Math.ceil(
    (checkIn.getTime() - today.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24),
  );

  const { bookableFromDaysBefore, bookableUntilDaysBefore } = dummySalesRule;

  if (diffDays > bookableFromDaysBefore) {
    return {
      code: 'BOOKING_TOO_EARLY',
      message: `莠育ｴ・女莉倥・${bookableFromDaysBefore}譌･蜑阪°繧峨〒縺吶Ａ,
      adminMessage: `蜿嶺ｻ倬幕蟋句燕: 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ${diffDays}譌･蠕・(蜿嶺ｻ倬幕蟋・{bookableFromDaysBefore}譌･蜑阪°繧・`,
    };
  }

  if (diffDays < bookableUntilDaysBefore) {
    return {
      code: 'BOOKING_TOO_LATE',
      message: `莠育ｴ・女莉倥・${bookableUntilDaysBefore}譌･蜑阪′邱蛻・〒縺吶Ａ,
      adminMessage: `蜿嶺ｻ倡ｷ蛻・ 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ${diffDays}譌･蠕・(邱蛻・{bookableUntilDaysBefore}譌･蜑阪∪縺ｧ)`,
    };
  }

  return null;
}

function checkClosedDates(
  checkInDate: string,
  checkOutDate: string,
): ValidationError | null {
  const stayDates = getStayDates(checkInDate, checkOutDate);
  const { closedDates } = dummySalesRule;

  const blocked = stayDates.filter((d) => closedDates.includes(d));
  if (blocked.length > 0) {
    return {
      code: 'CLOSED_DATE',
      message: '謖・ｮ壹＆繧後◆譌･遞九↓縺ｯ蜿嶺ｻ伜●豁｢譌･縺悟性縺ｾ繧後※縺・∪縺吶・,
      adminMessage: `蜿嶺ｻ伜●豁｢譌･: ${blocked.join(', ')}`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

function checkSiteClosureDates(
  siteNumber: string,
  checkInDate: string,
  checkOutDate: string,
): ValidationError | null {
  const stayDates = getStayDates(checkInDate, checkOutDate);
  const { siteClosures } = dummySalesRule;

  const closure = siteClosures.find((c) => c.siteNumber === siteNumber);
  if (!closure) return null;

  const blocked = stayDates.filter((d) => closure.dates.includes(d));
  if (blocked.length > 0) {
    return {
      code: 'SITE_CLOSED_DATE',
      message: `繧ｵ繧､繝・${siteNumber} 縺ｯ謖・ｮ壽律遞九〒蛻ｩ逕ｨ蛛懈ｭ｢荳ｭ縺ｧ縺吶Ａ,
      adminMessage: `繧ｵ繧､繝亥●豁｢: ${siteNumber} ${blocked.join(', ')} 逅・罰: ${closure.reason}`,
    };
  }
  return null;
}

// 笏笏笏 驥崎､・メ繧ｧ繝・け・磯撼蜷梧悄繝ｻSupabase・・笏笏笏

/**
 * 驥崎､・メ繧ｧ繝・け・磯撼蜷梧悄繝ｻSupabase・・
 *
 * 莉墓ｧ・ status='cancelled' 縺ｮ莠育ｴ・・驥崎､・愛螳壹・蟇ｾ雎｡螟悶→縺吶ｋ縲・
 * 螟画峩譎ゅ・ excludeId 縺ｫ閾ｪ蛻・・霄ｫ縺ｮ莠育ｴИD繧呈ｸ｡縺励∬・蟾ｱ驥崎､・ｒ蝗樣∩縺吶ｋ縲・
 */
async function checkOverlap(
  siteNumber: string,
  checkIn: string,
  checkOut: string,
  excludeId?: string,
): Promise<ValidationError | null> {
  let query = supabase
    .from('guest_reservations')
    .select('id, check_in_date, check_out_date')
    .eq('site_number', siteNumber)
    // cancelled 縺ｯ驥崎､・愛螳壼ｯｾ雎｡螟・
    .not('status', 'eq', 'cancelled')
    .lt('check_in_date', checkOut)
    .gt('check_out_date', checkIn)
    .limit(1);

  if (excludeId) {
    query = query.not('id', 'eq', excludeId);
  }

  const { data, error } = await query;

  if (error) {
    return {
      code: 'OVERLAP_CHECK_ERROR',
      message: '莠育ｴ・・驥崎､・｢ｺ隱堺ｸｭ縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲・,
      adminMessage: `驥崎､・メ繧ｧ繝・け繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ: ${error.message}`,
    };
  }

  if (data && data.length > 0) {
    const existing = data[0];
    return {
      code: 'DUPLICATE_RESERVATION',
      message: '縺疲欠螳壹・譌･遞九・縺吶〒縺ｫ莠育ｴ・′蜈･縺｣縺ｦ縺・∪縺吶ょ挨縺ｮ譌･遞九ｒ縺企∈縺ｳ縺上□縺輔＞縲・,
      adminMessage: `驥崎､・ 繧ｵ繧､繝・${siteNumber} 縺ｯ ${existing.check_in_date} 縲・${existing.check_out_date} 縺ｫ譌｢蟄倅ｺ育ｴ・(${existing.id}) 縺ゅｊ`,
    };
  }

  return null;
}

// 笏笏笏 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繝舌Μ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ髢｢謨ｰ 笏笏笏

/**
 * 莠育ｴ・ヰ繝ｪ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繧貞ｮ溯｡後☆繧九・
 *
 * 蜷梧悄繝√ぉ繝・け・域律莉倥・螳壼藤繝ｻ蜿嶺ｻ俶悄髢薙↑縺ｩ・俄・ 髱槫酔譛溘メ繧ｧ繝・け・磯㍾隍・ｼ峨・鬆・〒蜃ｦ逅・・
 * source 縺ｫ繧医▲縺ｦ荳驛ｨ繝√ぉ繝・け繧偵せ繧ｭ繝・・縺吶ｋ縲・
 *
 * @returns valid=true 縺ｪ繧峨お繝ｩ繝ｼ縺ｪ縺励Ｇalse 縺ｪ繧・errors 縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ驟榊・縲・
 */
export async function validateReservation(
  input: ReservationValidationInput,
): Promise<ValidationResult> {
  const errors: ValidationError[] = [];

  // --- 蜷梧悄繝√ぉ繝・け ---

  // 1. 譌･莉倬・ｺ・
  const dateErr = checkDateOrder(input);
  if (dateErr) {
    errors.push(dateErr);
    // 譌･莉倥′荳肴ｭ｣縺ｪ蝣ｴ蜷医∽ｻ･蠕後・繝√ぉ繝・け繧定｡後ｏ縺ｪ縺・
    return { valid: false, errors, nights: 0 };
  }

  // 2. 螳ｿ豕頑焚
  const nights = calculateNights(input.checkInDate, input.checkOutDate);

  const nightsErr = checkNightsRange(nights);
  if (nightsErr) errors.push(nightsErr);

  // 3. 莠ｺ謨ｰ繝√ぉ繝・け
  const guestsErr = checkGuestsPositive(input.guests);
  if (guestsErr) errors.push(guestsErr);

  // 4. 繧ｵ繧､繝亥ｭ伜惠遒ｺ隱・
  const siteErr = checkSiteExists(input.siteNumber);
  if (siteErr) {
    errors.push(siteErr);
    // 繧ｵ繧､繝医′蟄伜惠縺励↑縺・ｴ蜷医・縺ｿ縲√％縺薙〒謇薙■蛻・ｊ
    return { valid: false, errors, nights };
  }

  // 5. 繧ｵ繧､繝亥・髢九メ繧ｧ繝・け・・eb縺ｮ縺ｿ・・
  const sitePubErr = checkSitePublished(input.siteNumber, input.source);
  if (sitePubErr) errors.push(sitePubErr);

  // 6. 繧ｵ繧､繝医せ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ繝√ぉ繝・け
  const siteStatusErr = checkSiteStatus(input.siteNumber);
  if (siteStatusErr) errors.push(siteStatusErr);

  // 7. 螳壼藤繝√ぉ繝・け
  const capErr = checkCapacity(input.siteNumber, input.guests);
  if (capErr) errors.push(capErr);

  // 8. 繝励Λ繝ｳ蜈ｬ髢九メ繧ｧ繝・け・・eb縺ｮ縺ｿ・・
  const planErr = checkPlanPublished(input.planId, input.source);
  if (planErr) errors.push(planErr);

  // 9. 蜿嶺ｻ俶悄髢薙メ繧ｧ繝・け・・dmin縺ｯ繧ｹ繧ｭ繝・・・・
  const periodErr = checkBookingPeriod(input.checkInDate, input.source);
  if (periodErr) errors.push(periodErr);

  // 10. 蜿嶺ｻ伜●豁｢譌･繝√ぉ繝・け
  const closedErr = checkClosedDates(input.checkInDate, input.checkOutDate);
  if (closedErr) errors.push(closedErr);

  // 11. 繧ｵ繧､繝亥挨蛛懈ｭ｢譌･繝√ぉ繝・け
  const siteClosureErr = checkSiteClosureDates(
    input.siteNumber,
    input.checkInDate,
    input.checkOutDate,
  );
  if (siteClosureErr) errors.push(siteClosureErr);

  // 蜷梧悄繝√ぉ繝・け縺ｫ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺後≠繧後・髱槫酔譛溘メ繧ｧ繝・け縺ｯ繧ｹ繧ｭ繝・・
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return { valid: false, errors, nights };
  }

  // --- 髱槫酔譛溘メ繧ｧ繝・け ---

  // 12. 驥崎､・メ繧ｧ繝・け
  const overlapErr = await checkOverlap(
    input.siteNumber,
    input.checkInDate,
    input.checkOutDate,
    input.excludeReservationId,
  );
  if (overlapErr) errors.push(overlapErr);

  return {
    valid: errors.length === 0,
    errors,
    nights,
  };
}

/**
 * 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ驟榊・縺九ｉ繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ蜷代￠繝｡繝・そ繝ｼ繧ｸ繧帝｣邨・
 */
export function formatUserErrors(errors: ValidationError[]): string {
  return errors.map((e) => e.message).join('\n');
}

/**
 * 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ驟榊・縺九ｉ邂｡逅・・髄縺代Γ繝・そ繝ｼ繧ｸ繧帝｣邨・
 */
export function formatAdminErrors(errors: ValidationError[]): string {
  return errors.map((e) => `[${e.code}] ${e.adminMessage}`).join('\n');
}

import { createServerClient } from '@supabase/ssr';
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { isAdminEmail } from '@/lib/admin/auth';

export async function middleware(request: NextRequest) {
  const { pathname } = request.nextUrl;

  // /admin/login 縺ｯ隱崎ｨｼ荳崎ｦ・
  if (pathname === '/admin/login') {
    return await handleLoginPage(request);
  }

  // /admin 驟堺ｸ九・縺ｿ菫晁ｭｷ
  if (pathname.startsWith('/admin')) {
    return await protectAdmin(request);
  }

  return NextResponse.next();
}

/**
 * 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ繝壹・繧ｸ: 譌｢縺ｫ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ貂医∩邂｡逅・・↑繧・/admin 縺ｸ繝ｪ繝繧､繝ｬ繧ｯ繝・
 */
async function handleLoginPage(request: NextRequest) {
  const { supabase, response } = createMiddlewareClient(request);

  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();

  if (user && isAdminEmail(user.email)) {
    const url = request.nextUrl.clone();
    url.pathname = '/admin';
    return NextResponse.redirect(url, { headers: response.headers });
  }

  return response;
}

/**
 * /admin 驟堺ｸ九ｒ菫晁ｭｷ
 */
async function protectAdmin(request: NextRequest) {
  const { supabase, response } = createMiddlewareClient(request);

  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();

  // 譛ｪ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ 竊・/admin/login
  if (!user) {
    const url = request.nextUrl.clone();
    url.pathname = '/admin/login';
    url.searchParams.set('next', request.nextUrl.pathname);
    return NextResponse.redirect(url, { headers: response.headers });
  }

  // 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ貂医∩縺縺檎ｮ｡逅・・〒縺ｪ縺・竊・/admin/login?error=forbidden
  if (!isAdminEmail(user.email)) {
    const url = request.nextUrl.clone();
    url.pathname = '/admin/login';
    url.searchParams.set('error', 'forbidden');
    return NextResponse.redirect(url, { headers: response.headers });
  }

  return response;
}

/**
 * middleware 逕ｨ縺ｮ Supabase 繧ｯ繝ｩ繧､繧｢繝ｳ繝育函謌・
 */
function createMiddlewareClient(request: NextRequest) {
  let response = NextResponse.next({ request });

  const supabase = createServerClient(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        getAll() {
          return request.cookies.getAll();
        },
        setAll(cookiesToSet) {
          cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value }) =>
            request.cookies.set(name, value),
          );
          response = NextResponse.next({ request });
          cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value, options }) =>
            response.cookies.set(name, value, options),
          );
        },
      },
    },
  );

  return { supabase, response };
}

export const config = {
  matcher: ['/admin/:path*'],
};

export type BookingDraft = {
  stay: {
    checkIn: string | null;
    checkOut: string | null;
    nights: number;
    adults: number;
    children: number;
  };
  plan: {
    majorCategoryId: string | null;
    minorPlanId: string | null;
  };
  site: {
    areaId: string | null;
    siteId: string | null;
    siteNumber: string | null;
    siteName: string | null;
    sitePrice: number;
    siteFee: number;
    designationFee: number;
    areaName: string | null;
    subAreaName: string | null;
  };
  options: {
    rentals: Array<{
      optionId: string;
      quantity: number;
      days?: number;
      subtotal: number;
    }>;
    events: Array<{
      optionId: string;
      people: number;
      subtotal: number;
    }>;
  };
  policy: {
    agreedCancellation: boolean;
    agreedTerms: boolean;
    agreedSns: boolean;
  };
  payment: {
    method: "credit_card" | "on_site" | null;
  };
  meta: {
    version: number;
    updatedAt: number;
  };
};

type BookingDraftActions = {
  setStay: (stay: Partial<BookingDraft["stay"]>) => void;
  setPlan: (plan: Partial<BookingDraft["plan"]>) => void;
  resetPlan: () => void;
  setSite: (site: Partial<BookingDraft["site"]>) => void;
  setOptions: (options: Partial<BookingDraft["options"]>) => void;
  setPolicy: (policy: Partial<BookingDraft["policy"]>) => void;
  setPayment: (payment: Partial<BookingDraft["payment"]>) => void;
  reset: () => void;
};

/* 笏笏笏 蛻晄悄蛟､ 笏笏笏 */

const initialDraft: BookingDraft = {
  stay: {
    checkIn: null,
    checkOut: null,
    nights: 0,
    adults: 1,
    children: 0,
  },
  plan: {
    majorCategoryId: null,
    minorPlanId: null,
  },
  site: {
    areaId: null,
    siteId: null,
    siteNumber: null,
    siteName: null,
    sitePrice: 0,
    siteFee: 0,
    designationFee: 0,
    areaName: null,
    subAreaName: null,
  },
  options: {
    rentals: [],
    events: [],
  },
  policy: {
    agreedCancellation: false,
    agreedTerms: false,
    agreedSns: false,
  },
  payment: {
    method: null,
  },
  meta: {
    version: 1,
    updatedAt: 0,
  },
};

/* 笏笏笏 繧ｹ繝医い 笏笏笏 */

export const useBookingDraftStore = create<BookingDraft & BookingDraftActions>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      ...initialDraft,

      setStay: (stay) =>
        set((state) => ({
          stay: { ...state.stay, ...stay },
          meta: { ...state.meta, updatedAt: Date.now() },
        })),

      setPlan: (plan) =>
        set((state) => ({
          plan: { ...state.plan, ...plan },
          meta: { ...state.meta, updatedAt: Date.now() },
        })),

      resetPlan: () =>
        set((state) => ({
          plan: { ...initialDraft.plan },
          meta: { ...state.meta, updatedAt: Date.now() },
        })),

      setSite: (site) =>
        set((state) => ({
          site: { ...state.site, ...site },
          meta: { ...state.meta, updatedAt: Date.now() },
        })),

      setOptions: (options) =>
        set((state) => ({
          options: { ...state.options, ...options },
          meta: { ...state.meta, updatedAt: Date.now() },
        })),

      setPolicy: (policy) =>
        set((state) => ({
          policy: { ...state.policy, ...policy },
          meta: { ...state.meta, updatedAt: Date.now() },
        })),

      setPayment: (payment) =>
        set((state) => ({
          payment: { ...state.payment, ...payment },
          meta: { ...state.meta, updatedAt: Date.now() },
        })),

      reset: () =>
        set({ ...initialDraft, meta: { version: 1, updatedAt: Date.now() } }),
    }),
    {
      name: "booking-draft",
      storage: createJSONStorage(() => sessionStorage),
    },
  ),
);

import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist, createJSONStorage } from 'zustand/middleware';
import type { ImportHistoryEntry } from '@/types/importHistory';

const MAX_HISTORY = 50;

interface ImportHistoryState {
  entries: ImportHistoryEntry[];
  addEntry: (entry: ImportHistoryEntry) => void;
  clearAll: () => void;
}

export const useImportHistoryStore = create<ImportHistoryState>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      entries: [],

      addEntry: (entry) =>
        set((state) => ({
          entries: [entry, ...state.entries].slice(0, MAX_HISTORY),
        })),

      clearAll: () => set({ entries: [] }),
    }),
    {
      name: 'import-history',
      storage: createJSONStorage(() => localStorage),
    },
  ),
);

import type { Database } from './database';

type ReservationStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['reservation_status'];
type PaymentMethod = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_method'];
type PaymentStatus = Database['public']['Enums']['payment_status'];
type SiteType = Database['public']['Enums']['site_type'];

/** QR陦ｨ遉ｺ繝壹・繧ｸ縺ｧ菴ｿ逕ｨ縺吶ｋ莠育ｴ・ｩｳ邏ｰ縺ｮ邨ｱ蜷亥梛 */
export interface ReservationDetail {
  id: string;
  status: ReservationStatus;
  checkInDate: string;
  checkOutDate: string;
  guests: number;
  totalAmount: number;
  specialRequests: string | null;
  createdAt: string;

  // QR繧ｳ繝ｼ繝臥畑繝医・繧ｯ繝ｳ・亥ｰ・擂逧・↓鄂ｲ蜷堺ｻ倥″繝医・繧ｯ繝ｳ縺ｫ蟾ｮ縺玲崛縺亥庄閭ｽ・・
  qrToken: string;

  // 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ諠・ｱ
  checkedInAt: string | null;

  // 繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ諠・ｱ
  userName: string;
  userEmail: string;

  // 繧ｵ繧､繝域ュ蝣ｱ
  siteNumber: string;
  siteType: SiteType;

  // 繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ諠・ｱ
  campgroundName: string;

  // 豎ｺ貂域ュ蝣ｱ
  paymentMethod: PaymentMethod | null;
  paymentStatus: PaymentStatus | null;
}

/** 蜿嶺ｻ倥さ繝ｼ繝臥函謌千畑繝倥Ν繝代・・・eservation_id縺ｮ蜈磯ｭ8譁・ｭ励ｒ螟ｧ譁・ｭ怜喧・・*/
export function generateReceptionCode(reservationId: string): string {
  return reservationId.replace(/-/g, '').substring(0, 8).toUpperCase();
}

/** 螳ｿ豕頑焚繧定ｨ育ｮ・*/
export function calculateNights(checkIn: string, checkOut: string): number {
  const inDate = new Date(checkIn);
  const outDate = new Date(checkOut);
  return Math.ceil((outDate.getTime() - inDate.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
}

/** 繧ｵ繧､繝医ち繧､繝励・譌･譛ｬ隱槭Λ繝吶Ν */
export function getSiteTypeLabel(type: SiteType): string {
  const labels: Record<SiteType, string> = {
    standard: '繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ繝・,
    premium: '繝励Ξ繝溘い繝',
    deluxe: '繝・Λ繝・け繧ｹ',
    tent_only: '繝・Φ繝亥ｰら畑',

/** 謾ｯ謇輔＞譁ｹ豕輔・譌･譛ｬ隱槭Λ繝吶Ν */
export function getPaymentMethodLabel(method: PaymentMethod | null): string {
  if (!method) return '譛ｪ險ｭ螳・;
  const labels: Record<PaymentMethod, string> = {
    credit_card: '繧ｯ繝ｬ繧ｸ繝・ヨ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝・,
    cash: '迴ｾ蝨ｰ謇輔＞',
    bank_transfer: '驫陦梧険霎ｼ',
  };
  return labels[method];
}

/** 謾ｯ謇輔＞繧ｹ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ縺ｮ譌･譛ｬ隱槭Λ繝吶Ν */

  if (!status) return '譛ｪ險ｭ螳・;
  const labels: Record<PaymentStatus, string> = {
    pending: '豎ｺ貂亥ｾ・■',
    paid: '豎ｺ貂域ｸ医∩',
    refunded: '霑秘≡貂医∩',
    failed: '豎ｺ貂亥､ｱ謨・,
  };
  return labels[status];
}

-- Enable UUID extension
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- Create custom types
CREATE TYPE reservation_status AS ENUM ('pending', 'confirmed', 'checked_in', 'completed', 'cancelled');
CREATE TYPE payment_status AS ENUM ('pending', 'paid', 'refunded', 'failed');
CREATE TYPE payment_method AS ENUM ('credit_card', 'cash', 'bank_transfer');
CREATE TYPE site_type AS ENUM ('standard', 'premium', 'deluxe', 'tent_only', 'rv_only');
CREATE TYPE user_role AS ENUM ('user', 'admin', 'manager');

-- Create users table (extends Supabase auth.users)
CREATE TABLE public.profiles (
  id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE PRIMARY KEY,
  email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  phone TEXT,
  full_name TEXT,
  role user_role DEFAULT 'user',
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL
);

-- Create campgrounds table
CREATE TABLE public.campgrounds (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  address TEXT,
  phone TEXT,
  email TEXT,
  capacity INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  operating_hours JSONB, -- {monday: {open: "08:00", close: "18:00"}}
  amenities JSONB, -- ["wifi", "showers", "laundry"]
  rules TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL
);

-- Create sites table
CREATE TABLE public.sites (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  campground_id UUID REFERENCES public.campgrounds(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  site_number TEXT NOT NULL,
  type site_type DEFAULT 'standard',
  capacity INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 4, -- max guests
  price_per_night DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  features JSONB, -- {water: true, electricity: true, sewer: false}
  location_data JSONB, -- {lat: 35.123, lng: 139.456, elevation: 100}
  drainage_rating INTEGER CHECK (drainage_rating >= 1 AND drainage_rating <= 5), -- 1-5 scale
  slope_rating INTEGER CHECK (slope_rating >= 1 AND slope_rating <= 5), -- 1-5 scale
  view_rating INTEGER CHECK (view_rating >= 1 AND view_rating <= 5), -- 1-5 scale
  distance_to_facilities INTEGER, -- meters
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,

  UNIQUE(campground_id, site_number)
);

-- Create options table (additional services)
CREATE TABLE public.options (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  price DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL
);

-- Create reservations table
CREATE TABLE public.reservations (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES public.profiles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  site_id UUID REFERENCES public.sites(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  check_in_date DATE NOT NULL,
  check_out_date DATE NOT NULL,
  guests INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  total_amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
  status reservation_status DEFAULT 'pending',
  special_requests TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,

  CHECK (check_out_date > check_in_date),
  CHECK (guests > 0)
);

-- Create reservation_options junction table
CREATE TABLE public.reservation_options (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES public.reservations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  option_id UUID REFERENCES public.options(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  quantity INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,

  UNIQUE(reservation_id, option_id)
);

-- Create payments table
CREATE TABLE public.payments (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES public.reservations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
  currency TEXT DEFAULT 'JPY',
  method payment_method DEFAULT 'credit_card',
  status payment_status DEFAULT 'pending',
  stripe_payment_intent_id TEXT,
  stripe_charge_id TEXT,
  paid_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL
);

-- Create check_ins table
CREATE TABLE public.check_ins (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES public.reservations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  checked_in_by UUID REFERENCES public.profiles(id),
  check_in_time TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  qr_code TEXT UNIQUE,
  notes TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL
);

-- Create notifications table
CREATE TABLE public.notifications (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES public.profiles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES public.reservations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'booking_confirmed', 'reminder', 'check_in_ready'
  title TEXT NOT NULL,
  message TEXT NOT NULL,
  sent_via JSONB, -- {email: true, line: false}
  sent_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL
);

RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
  NEW.updated_at = TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW());
  RETURN NEW;
END;

-- Create function to check site availability
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.check_site_availability(
  p_site_id UUID,
  p_check_in DATE,
  p_check_out DATE
) RETURNS BOOLEAN AS $$
BEGIN
  RETURN NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM public.reservations
    WHERE site_id = p_site_id
      AND status NOT IN ('cancelled')
      AND (
        (check_in_date <= p_check_in AND check_out_date > p_check_in) OR
        (check_in_date < p_check_out AND check_out_date >= p_check_out) OR
        (check_in_date >= p_check_in AND check_out_date <= p_check_out)
      )
  );
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

-- Create function to calculate total reservation amount
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.calculate_reservation_total(
  p_site_id UUID,
  p_check_in DATE,
  p_check_out DATE,
  p_option_ids UUID[] DEFAULT ARRAY[]::UUID[]
) RETURNS DECIMAL(10,2) AS $$
DECLARE
  nights_count INTEGER;
  site_price DECIMAL(10,2);
  options_total DECIMAL(10,2) := 0;
  total DECIMAL(10,2);
BEGIN
  -- Calculate number of nights
  nights_count := p_check_out - p_check_in;

  -- Get site price
  SELECT price_per_night INTO site_price
  FROM public.sites
  WHERE id = p_site_id;

  -- Calculate options total
  IF array_length(p_option_ids, 1) > 0 THEN
    SELECT COALESCE(SUM(price), 0) INTO options_total
    FROM public.options
    WHERE id = ANY(p_option_ids);
  END IF;

  -- Calculate total
  total := (site_price * nights_count) + options_total;

  RETURN total;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

  error_message TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL,
  sent_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
);

CREATE INDEX idx_notification_logs_reservation ON public.notification_logs(reservation_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_notification_logs_created ON public.notification_logs(created_at DESC);

-- admin_action_logs: 邂｡逅・・桃菴懊Ο繧ｰ
CREATE TABLE public.admin_action_logs (
  id UUID DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4() PRIMARY KEY,
  admin_email TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  action_type TEXT NOT NULL,
  target_type TEXT NOT NULL,
  target_id TEXT,
  before_json JSONB,
  after_json JSONB,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT TIMEZONE('utc'::text, NOW()) NOT NULL
);

CREATE INDEX idx_admin_action_logs_created ON public.admin_action_logs(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_admin_action_logs_target ON public.admin_action_logs(target_type, target_id);

-- RLS
ALTER TABLE public.notification_logs ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE public.admin_action_logs ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "notification_logs_anon_all" ON public.notification_logs
  FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

CREATE POLICY "admin_action_logs_anon_all" ON public.admin_action_logs
  FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- guest_reservations 縺ｫ莠ｺ謨ｰ蜀・ｨｳ繝ｻ繝壹ャ繝医・霆雁床謨ｰ繧ｫ繝ｩ繝繧定ｿｽ蜉
-- 譌｢蟄倥・ guests 繧ｫ繝ｩ繝縺ｯ蜷郁ｨ井ｺｺ謨ｰ縺ｨ縺励※谿九☆・亥ｾ梧婿莠呈鋤・・

ALTER TABLE public.guest_reservations
  ADD COLUMN adults   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  ADD COLUMN children INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN infants  INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN pets     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN cars     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

-- RLS: 譌｢蟄倥・繝ｪ繧ｷ繝ｼ縺ｧ UPDATE 繧定ｨｱ蜿ｯ縺励※縺・↑縺・ｴ蜷医↓霑ｽ蜉
DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_policies
    WHERE tablename = 'guest_reservations' AND policyname = 'Allow anonymous update'
  ) THEN
    CREATE POLICY "Allow anonymous update" ON public.guest_reservations
      FOR UPDATE USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
  END IF;
END$$;

# 繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ莠育ｴ・す繧ｹ繝・Β - 繝・・繧ｿ繝吶・繧ｹ險ｭ險・

## ER蝗ｳ

```mermaid
erDiagram
    profiles ||--o{ reservations : "makes"
    profiles ||--o{ check_ins : "performs"
    profiles ||--o{ notifications : "receives"

    campgrounds ||--o{ sites : "contains"
    sites ||--o{ reservations : "has"

    reservations ||--o{ reservation_options : "includes"
    reservations ||--o{ payments : "has"
    reservations ||--o{ check_ins : "has"
    reservations ||--o{ notifications : "triggers"

    options ||--o{ reservation_options : "selected_in"

    profiles {
        uuid id PK
        text email UK
        text phone
        text full_name
        user_role role
        timestamp created_at
        timestamp updated_at
    }

    campgrounds {
        uuid id PK
        text name
        text description
        text address
        text phone
        text email
        integer capacity
        jsonb operating_hours
        jsonb amenities
        text rules
        timestamp created_at
        timestamp updated_at
    }

    sites {
        uuid id PK
        uuid campground_id FK
        text site_number UK
        site_type type
        integer capacity
        decimal price_per_night
        text description
        jsonb features
        jsonb location_data
        integer drainage_rating
        integer slope_rating
        integer view_rating
        integer distance_to_facilities
        boolean is_active
        timestamp created_at
        timestamp updated_at
    }

    options {
        uuid id PK
        text name
        text description
        decimal price
        boolean is_active
        timestamp created_at
        timestamp updated_at
    }

    reservations {
        uuid id PK
        uuid user_id FK
        uuid site_id FK
        date check_in_date
        date check_out_date
        integer guests
        decimal total_amount
        reservation_status status
        text special_requests
        timestamp created_at
        timestamp updated_at
    }

    reservation_options {
        uuid id PK
        uuid reservation_id FK
        uuid option_id FK
        integer quantity
        timestamp created_at
    }

    payments {
        uuid id PK
        uuid reservation_id FK
        decimal amount
        text currency
        payment_method method
        payment_status status
        text stripe_payment_intent_id
        text stripe_charge_id
        timestamp paid_at
        timestamp created_at
        timestamp updated_at
    }

    check_ins {
        uuid id PK
        uuid reservation_id FK
        uuid checked_in_by FK
        timestamp check_in_time
        text qr_code UK
        text notes
        timestamp created_at
    }

    notifications {
        uuid id PK
        uuid user_id FK
        uuid reservation_id FK
        text type
        text title
        text message
        jsonb sent_via
        timestamp sent_at
        timestamp created_at
    }
```

## 繝・・繝悶Ν隧ｳ邏ｰ

### 荳ｻ隕√お繝ｳ繝・ぅ繝・ぅ

#### profiles (繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ諠・ｱ)
- Supabase Auth 縺ｨ騾｣謳ｺ
- 繝ｭ繝ｼ繝ｫ繝吶・繧ｹ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ蛻ｶ蠕｡・・ser/admin/manager・・

#### campgrounds (繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ)
- 蝓ｺ譛ｬ諠・ｱ縺ｨ險ｭ蛯呎ュ蝣ｱ
- JSONB 縺ｧ譟碑ｻ溘↑繝・・繧ｿ讒矩

#### sites (繧ｵ繧､繝・
- 蜷・く繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ縺ｮ蛹ｺ逕ｻ諠・ｱ
- 隧ｳ邏ｰ縺ｪ隧穂ｾ｡繝・・繧ｿ・域ｰｴ縺ｯ縺代・蛯ｾ譁懊・譎ｯ隕ｳ・・
- 菴咲ｽｮ諠・ｱ縺ｨ險ｭ蛯呎ュ蝣ｱ

#### reservations (莠育ｴ・
- 莠育ｴ・・譬ｸ蠢・ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ
- 譌･莉倬㍾隍・メ繧ｧ繝・け蠢・・
- 繧ｹ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ邂｡逅・

#### options (繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ繧ｵ繝ｼ繝薙せ)
- 繧｢繝ｼ繝ｪ繝ｼ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ縲√・繝・ヨ譁咎≡縺ｪ縺ｩ
- 蜍慕噪萓｡譬ｼ險ｭ螳・

### 髢｢菫ゅユ繝ｼ繝悶Ν

#### reservation_options (莠育ｴ・が繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ)
- 螟壼ｯｾ螟夐未菫ゅ・隗｣豎ｺ
- 謨ｰ驥乗欠螳壼庄閭ｽ

#### payments (豎ｺ貂・
- Stripe 邨ｱ蜷育畑
- 隍・焚豎ｺ貂域婿蠑丞ｯｾ蠢・

#### check_ins (繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ)
- QR繧ｳ繝ｼ繝牙ｯｾ蠢・
- 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ螻･豁ｴ

#### notifications (騾夂衍)
- 繝｡繝ｼ繝ｫ/LINE 騾夂衍邂｡逅・
- 騾∽ｿ｡螻･豁ｴ霑ｽ霍｡

## 繧ｻ繧ｭ繝･繝ｪ繝・ぅ險ｭ險・

- 繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ・夊・霄ｫ縺ｮ繝・・繧ｿ縺ｮ縺ｿ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ
- 邂｡逅・・ｼ壼・繝・・繧ｿ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ
- 蜈ｬ髢九ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ・壹く繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ繝ｻ繧ｵ繧､繝域ュ蝣ｱ

### 繝薙ず繝阪せ繝ｫ繝ｼ繝ｫ
- 繧ｵ繧､繝磯㍾隍・ｺ育ｴ・亟豁｢
- 驥鷹｡崎ｨ育ｮ鈴未謨ｰ
- 蝨ｨ蠎ｫ繝√ぉ繝・け髢｢謨ｰ

# Campsite Booking SaaS

繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ縺ｮ莠育ｴ・懊メ繧ｧ繝・け繧､繝ｳ縺ｾ縺ｧ繧貞ｮ悟・閾ｪ蜍募喧縺吶ｋWeb繧｢繝励Μ繧ｱ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繝励Λ繝・ヨ繝輔か繝ｼ繝縲・
## 噫 讎りｦ・
- **莠育ｴ・･ｭ蜍吶・閾ｪ蜍募喧**: 莠ｺ莉ｶ雋ｻ蜑頑ｸ帙→UX蜷台ｸ翫ｒ螳溽樟
- **LINE騾｣謳ｺ**: 螟夜Κ繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ縺九ｉ縺ｮ豬∝・縺ｧ莠育ｴ・ｰ守ｷ壹ｒ譛驕ｩ蛹・- **QR繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ**: 髱樊磁隗ｦ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ縺ｧ蜉ｹ邇・喧
- **繝槭Ν繝√く繝｣繝ｳ繝怜ｴ蟇ｾ蠢・*: 蟆・擂逧・↑莠区･ｭ諡｡螟ｧ繧定ｦ区紺縺医◆險ｭ險・
## 屏・・謚陦薙せ繧ｿ繝・け

- **Frontend**: Next.js 16 (App Router)
- **Backend**: Supabase (PostgreSQL + Auth + Storage)
- **豎ｺ貂・*: Stripe
- **騾夂衍**: LINE Messaging API (蟆・擂諡｡蠑ｵ)
- **險隱・*: TypeScript
- **繧ｹ繧ｿ繧､繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｰ**: Tailwind CSS
- **LINE LIFF**: LINE繧｢繝励Μ蜀・eb繧｢繝励Μ

## 搭 讖溯・荳隕ｧ

### 繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ讖溯・
- 笨・譌･莉倥・莠ｺ謨ｰ驕ｸ謚・- 笨・繧ｵ繧､繝磯∈謚朸I・亥ｺｧ蟶ｭ謖・ｮ夲ｼ・- 笨・繧ｪ繝励す繝ｧ繝ｳ驕ｸ謚橸ｼ医い繝ｼ繝ｪ繝ｼ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ遲会ｼ・- 笨・豎ｺ貂茨ｼ・tripe繧ｯ繝ｬ繧ｸ繝・ヨ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨∫樟蝨ｰ豎ｺ貂茨ｼ・- 笨・莠育ｴ・｢ｺ隱阪・騾夂衍
- 笨・LINE LIFF繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ
- 笨・QR繧ｳ繝ｼ繝峨メ繧ｧ繝・け繧､繝ｳ

### 邂｡逅・・ｩ溯・
- 笨・莠育ｴ・ｸ隕ｧ繝ｻ邂｡逅・- 笨・繧ｵ繧､繝域ュ蝣ｱ邂｡逅・ｼ域ｰｴ縺ｯ縺代・蛯ｾ譁懊・譎ｯ隕ｳ・・- 笨・CSV繧ｨ繧ｯ繧ｹ繝昴・繝・- 笨・謇句虚莠育ｴ・ｿｽ蜉
- 笨・邂｡逅・判髱｢ (`/admin`)

### 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ讖溯・
- 笨・QR繧ｳ繝ｼ繝峨メ繧ｧ繝・け繧､繝ｳ (`/checkin?id=xxx`)
- 笨・繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ譎る俣險倬鹸
- 笨・繧ｹ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ譖ｴ譁ｰ

## 噫 繧ｻ繝・ヨ繧｢繝・・

### 1. 繝ｪ繝昴ず繝医Μ縺ｮ繧ｯ繝ｭ繝ｼ繝ｳ
```bash
git clone <repository-url>
cd campsite-booking
```

### 2. 萓晏ｭ倬未菫ゅ・繧､繝ｳ繧ｹ繝医・繝ｫ
```bash
npm install
```

### 3. 迺ｰ蠅・､画焚縺ｮ險ｭ螳・`.env.local` 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ繧剃ｽ懈・縺励∽ｻ･荳九・蛟､繧定ｨｭ螳夲ｼ・
```env
# Supabase
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=your_supabase_url_here
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=your_supabase_anon_key_here
SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY=your_supabase_service_role_key_here

# Stripe
NEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=pk_test_your_stripe_publishable_key_here
STRIPE_SECRET_KEY=sk_test_your_stripe_secret_key_here
STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET=whsec_your_webhook_secret_here

# LINE LIFF
NEXT_PUBLIC_LINE_LIFF_ID=your_line_liff_id_here

# LINE Messaging API (蟆・擂諡｡蠑ｵ逕ｨ)
LINE_CHANNEL_ACCESS_TOKEN=your_line_channel_access_token_here
LINE_CHANNEL_SECRET=your_line_channel_secret_here
```

### 4. 繝・・繧ｿ繝吶・繧ｹ縺ｮ繧ｻ繝・ヨ繧｢繝・・
Supabase繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医ｒ菴懈・縺励∽ｻ･荳九・SQL繧貞ｮ溯｡鯉ｼ・
```bash
supabase db push
```

縺ｾ縺溘・縲√・繧､繧ｰ繝ｬ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ繧貞ｮ溯｡鯉ｼ・```bash
supabase migration up
```

### 5. 髢狗匱繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・縺ｮ襍ｷ蜍・```bash
npm run dev
```

繝悶Λ繧ｦ繧ｶ縺ｧ `http://localhost:3000` 縺ｫ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ縲・
## 導 LINE LIFF 險ｭ螳・
1. LINE Developers Console 縺ｧ LIFF 繧｢繝励Μ繧剃ｽ懈・
2. LIFF ID 繧貞叙蠕励＠縺ｦ迺ｰ蠅・､画焚縺ｫ險ｭ螳・3. Endpoint URL 繧・`https://your-domain.com` 縺ｫ險ｭ螳・4. 蠢・ｦ√↓蠢懊§縺ｦ繧ｹ繧ｳ繝ｼ繝励ｒ險ｭ螳夲ｼ・rofile, openid・・
## 諜 Stripe 險ｭ螳・
1. Stripe Dashboard 縺ｧ繧｢繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝井ｽ懈・
2. API繧ｭ繝ｼ繧貞叙蠕励＠縺ｦ迺ｰ蠅・､画焚縺ｫ險ｭ螳・3. Webhook 繧ｨ繝ｳ繝峨・繧､繝ｳ繝医ｒ險ｭ螳夲ｼ域ｱｺ貂亥ｮ御ｺ・夂衍逕ｨ・・
## 肌 繝薙Ν繝峨・繝・・繝ｭ繧､

### 繝薙Ν繝・```bash
npm run build
```

### 繝励Ο繝繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繝・・繝ｭ繧､
```bash
npm start
```

Vercel, Netlify 遲峨・繝励Λ繝・ヨ繝輔か繝ｼ繝縺ｫ繝・・繝ｭ繧､蜿ｯ閭ｽ縲・
## 唐 繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝域ｧ矩

```

笏・  笏披楳笏 layout.tsx         # 繝ｫ繝ｼ繝医Ξ繧､繧｢繧ｦ繝・笏懌楳笏 components/            # 蜀榊茜逕ｨ繧ｳ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・笏・  笏懌楳笏 QRCodeDisplay.tsx # QR繧ｳ繝ｼ繝芽｡ｨ遉ｺ

    笏披楳笏 database.ts        # DB蝙句ｮ夂ｾｩ

## ､・雋｢迪ｮ

1. Fork 縺吶ｋ
2. Feature 繝悶Λ繝ｳ繝√ｒ菴懈・ (`git checkout -b feature/amazing-feature`)
3. 繧ｳ繝溘ャ繝医☆繧・(`git commit -m 'Add amazing feature'`)
4. Push 縺吶ｋ (`git push origin feature/amazing-feature`)
5. Pull Request 繧剃ｽ懈・

## 塘 繝ｩ繧､繧ｻ繝ｳ繧ｹ

縺薙・繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医・ MIT 繝ｩ繧､繧ｻ繝ｳ繧ｹ縺ｮ荳九〒蜈ｬ髢九＆繧後※縺・∪縺吶・- `check_ins` - 繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ螻･豁ｴ

## 噫 髢狗匱迺ｰ蠅・そ繝・ヨ繧｢繝・・

### 1. 萓晏ｭ倬未菫ゅう繝ｳ繧ｹ繝医・繝ｫ
```bash
npm install
```

### 2. 迺ｰ蠅・､画焚險ｭ螳・```bash
cp .env.example .env.local
```

莉･荳九・迺ｰ蠅・､画焚繧定ｨｭ螳壹＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞・・- Supabase URL & Keys
- Stripe Keys
- LINE API Keys (蟆・擂諡｡蠑ｵ逕ｨ)

### 3. Supabase 繝槭う繧ｰ繝ｬ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ螳溯｡・```bash
# Supabase CLI 縺後う繝ｳ繧ｹ繝医・繝ｫ縺輔ｌ縺ｦ縺・ｋ蝣ｴ蜷・supabase db push
```

縺ｾ縺溘・縲ヾupabase Dashboard 縺九ｉ繝槭う繧ｰ繝ｬ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳSQL繧呈焔蜍募ｮ溯｡後・
### 4. 髢狗匱繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・襍ｷ蜍・```bash
npm run dev
```

## 白 繧ｻ繧ｭ繝･繝ｪ繝・ぅ

- Row Level Security (RLS) 縺ｫ繧医ｋ繝・・繧ｿ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ蛻ｶ蠕｡
- 繝医Λ繝ｳ繧ｶ繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ縺ｫ繧医ｋ蜷梧凾莠育ｴ・ｫｶ蜷磯亟豁｢
- 豎ｺ貂域ュ蝣ｱ縺ｮ螳牙・縺ｪ蜃ｦ逅・ｼ・tripe・・
